align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拉珍（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村村妇，是扎陵湖乡河源新村南杰家族的女儿，已婚育有两个孩子，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>岁的女儿名叫塔嘎，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>岁的儿子名叫次嘉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">7</span>连<span lang="EN-US">28</span>号公民，哈萨克族穆斯林，清真寺伊玛目（政府指定的穆斯林领祷人），中国在押良心犯。自新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克族等少数族裔被中共新疆当局高压严控，采取集中教育培训（又称“再教育营”）以来，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年是被当局以各种罪由送“再教育营”，而后被再转拘捕、判刑最多的一年；腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔虽为中共官方指定的伊斯兰教伊玛目（领祷人），也从未参加任何宗教极端势力，但<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，却被察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团派出所警突然带走，并送某“再教育营”接受洗脑式培训（实则关押）；后因强行教育培训过程中不与官方妥协、合作，遂于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月之后，被察布查尔县警方刑拘和逮捕，指控其“念经（古兰经）即违法”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年下半年（具体日期不详），其案在犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县法院正式开庭审理受理，最终在无代理辩护律师及家人在场的情况下，被以“念古兰经”罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">23</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2041</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。目前在新疆生产建设兵团第七师奎屯监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/23.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/23.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">兰太莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆市江北区法院对七十二岁的法轮功学员，女，家住重庆市合川区。曾遭看守所、洗脑班迫害　非法判刑一年缓两年。在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两天，各使用一张印有“法轮大法好 真善忍好”的纸币购物，并拥有法轮功真相资料，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日遭重庆江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">郎计云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西省忻州市代县法轮功女学员，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，她突然遭受到代县公安局抄家、抓捕，在抄家过程中只搜查到<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个真相光盘，就以此为借口把郎计云抓捕到代县洗脑班进行迫害，她一直给相关参与迫害的邪党人员讲真相，不配合邪恶的要求。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被代县公安局执行逮捕，关押在忻州市看守所迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并且罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445961.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，郎淑英被开庭，因为中共法院暗箱作业，违法操作，不通知家人，仅得知她可能被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后被关押河北省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日获悉，郎淑英因坚持信仰，坚持炼法轮功，以及不戴犯人标牌，被狱警和犯人迫害。由于家人无力帮助她，狱中的她经济困难，连卫生纸都没有钱买。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/27/2022-6-27.html#zip4"><b <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">赖成妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东省清远市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，家住广东省清远连州市连州镇鹅公潭村。此前，因宣传法轮功，赖成妹<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被拘禁十五天，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，广东省清远市连州市警察大规模抓捕法轮功学员，当地邵艳芳、赖成妹等<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位法轮功学员被抓捕。邵艳芳、赖成妹被关押到阳山县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。被构陷到英德市检察院后，邵艳芳、赖成妹被转移到英德市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，邵艳芳被英德市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；赖成妹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元。赖成妹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">雷小利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西西安市辛家庙法轮功学员，女，她双眼近乎失明，日常生活需靠家人帮助。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，雷小利被莲湖区大莲花池派出所警察，以所谓的“在取款机上放小册子”为名，抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，她被关押在西安莲湖区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，雷小利被莲湖区法院开庭。庭上，维权律师为雷小利做了无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，家属接到雷小利被莲湖区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千的通知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip6"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip6</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">雷云波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，原荆州银行系统职工。因修炼法轮功被单位开除。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年在河南发真相资料被抓捕，后在武汉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。在范家台监狱被殴打，被超体力奴役。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年初，雷云波在云南被抓捕后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬，雷云波又被抓捕，至今仍被关押在荆州市沙市区看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">长春法轮功学员。冷凤翎女士目前被关押在吉林省女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日家人去监狱会见，才得知她被判处刑期<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被长春路园区国保、公安分局、长春和平大街派出所联合抓捕，并抄家，随后冷凤翎被刑事拘留，关押在第四看守所。现在冷凤翎被非法关押在吉林省女子监狱，构陷她的罪名是所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”，目前在第八监区第五支队，人员编号：<span lang="EN-US">70010194</span>。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">楞珠扎巴（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏歌手。楞珠扎巴于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被拘留，距离他<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月发行歌曲“黑帽子”不到两个月。在经过一年多的审前拘留之后，他于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑，被剥夺了辩护判权。楞珠扎巴最终判处<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年徒刑，理由是他在西藏那曲市比如县演唱批评政府镇压政策的歌曲。此前，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，楞珠扎巴与另一位著名的藏族歌手贡布丹增合唱一首名为《扎西央卓》的歌曲，其内容阐释境内藏人在中国政府的压制下遭受的状况和赞颂达赖喇嘛尊者，贡布丹增最终于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判处三年半徒刑。楞珠扎巴曾被监禁在那格监狱，目前他所监禁的位置和健康状况尚未清楚。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李佰华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨著名民主人士于云峰妻子。于云峰、李佰华夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭哈尔滨市公安局香坊分局以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。本次夫妇一起被拘留具体事因未明。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉于云峰、李佰华夫妇均被以寻衅滋事罪名，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月（二审）被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，李佰华于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份已移送黑龙江女子监狱（集训队）服刑。于云峰目前还关押于哈尔滨香坊区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李保兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市武清区豆张庄镇周立营村法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>女，<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李保兰、齐文伯在发放法轮功资料时被豆张庄镇派出所警察抓捕并抄家。由于身体原因（血压高），她们被以取保候审的名义放回家中。但<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多来，公检法相关人员一直在构陷她们。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日左右，李保兰、齐文伯先后被开庭。李保兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，齐文伯被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，但在庭审判决后她们安全回家了。可在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她们被豆张庄派出所警察与法院执行庭的人，强行从家中抓捕到武清看守所关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/25/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%A4%E4%BD%8D%E8%80%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%A6%87%E5%A5%B3%E6%9D%8E%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E9%BD%90%E6%96%87%E4%BC%AF%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-452342.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/25/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%A4%E4%BD%8D%E8%80%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%A6%87%E5%A5%B3%E6%9D%8E%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E9%BD%90%E6%96%87%E4%BC%AF%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-452342.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李本才：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，安徽省宿州市人，宿州市埇桥区三八街道宿涡路拂晓一号安置区<span lang="EN-US">14</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">203</span>室公民，强拆受害者，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年以来，因其果园被当地政府侵占、房屋遭强拆，多次投诉而无果，遂被迫走上漫漫维权上访路；期间，因屡次进京信访维权、讨公道，曾多次被拘留，而其合法维权赔偿要求一直得不到合理解决；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾就果园被侵占和房屋遭强拆事宜向法院提起行政赔偿诉讼，但最终被宿州市中级法院驳回；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因与其胞弟李本业以及另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名维权访民一起到安徽省宿州市信访局和宿州市法院大门口拉横幅，抗议法院就他们的信访案件枉法裁判、制造冤假错案，次日，遂<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均遭当地派出所警方传唤，并给予行政拘留处罚；后其与其弟未被送入拘留所，在被扣押<span lang="EN-US">8</span>小时后终获释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，因又到宿州市信访局上访，要求解决其果园被侵占、房屋被强拆以及赔偿补足款长期未得解决等问题，宿州市信访局随即就将其要求申请又转给埇桥区信访局，遂其不得不再到区政府，并对接待官员说：“若区政府仍不给解决问题，就将到北京找党给解决”；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，突然被宿州市埇桥区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓走刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被宿州市埇桥区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天之后，其案被埇桥区公安局向埇桥区检察院移送起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案一审在安徽省宿州市埇桥区法院开庭审理，后被以“寻衅滋事罪”速判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日；其不服，上诉；二审正在等待中；据悉，其被速判疑与“二十大”即将召开，当局需要维稳有关。目前被羁押于宿州市泗县看守所（安徽省宿州市泗县阀北路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">234300</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/210.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/210.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 65.35pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北泊头市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，河南警察闯到李彬家，把他的家翻了个底朝天，理由是；李彬在手机上发了中共当局不喜欢的信息。当天就把他抓捕至河南，后给他安上一个“利用×教组织破坏法律实施罪”罪名，对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款五万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/18/449740.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/18/449740.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林长春市农安县青山乡法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生。李聪女士<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在自家的油房被青山乡派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到农安县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李聪接到判决书，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚金两万元。李聪不服判决，上诉到长春市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，长春市中级法院未经开庭就宣布维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，李聪被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续关押迫害。入监后，每天晚上十二点睡、三点就被强制起来，坐小板凳。狱警纵容犯人虐待她，经常不给主食只给发糕、咸菜，逼强迫转化。在狱中，李聪一直遭受种种折磨：长时间罚站、饿刑、熬鹰、坐小凳、不准洗漱、围攻「洗脑」、人格侮辱等迫害外，还受到殴打，大冬天还开窗冻她，往她身上泼冷水。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李大尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省荆州市监利县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十六岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午十一点左右，监利县国保大队、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、县公安局、特警出动大量警力，在同一时间合谋抓捕了李大尧、李乐成、朱春新、何成、王升贵五位法轮功学员，不由分说直接把人从家里带走，紧接着非法抄家，家中被翻得一片狼藉，电脑等大量私人物品被全部抢走，没留下什么清单。其中李大尧家的门被警察请来的撬锁人强行撬开。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。后上诉，荆州中级法院维持原判。李大尧<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被劫持到在湖北省范家台监狱关押。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李德宽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省蛟河市法河沿村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>，李德宽在蛟河市长安街的出租房内被街道派出所警察绑架，并遭非法抄家，其中有三套师父法像和很多大法书籍，家中九万五千余元现金也被警察拿走。五月一日下午，李德宽被押送到蛟河市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李德宽被吉林省蛟河市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李德香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃金昌市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年出生，家住甘肃省金昌市。在中共对法轮功持续迫害的<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年中，累计被监禁<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午，李德香在家中被滨河路派出所、龙津里社区人员抓捕，被关押在金昌市金川区看守所，后得知已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/28/%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E9%87%91%E6%98%8C%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E5%BE%B7%E9%A6%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434127.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/28/%E7%94%98%E8%82%83%E9%87%91%E6%98%8C%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E5%BE%B7%E9%A6%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-434127.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李东军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林松原市前郭县红光农场九分场法轮功学员。李东军、黄秀华夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚七点多被松原市国保大队抓捕抄家。家里被抄走多部手机，两本《转法轮》、《洪吟五》一本，台历一个，对联一对，一个炼功播放器。后被关押在松原市善友看守所，最近得知他已经被庭审，李东军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现被关押在四平市公主岭监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李东哲（朝鲜）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，朝鲜族，辽阳市朝阳村基督教家庭教会负责人、牧师，良心犯。因中共当局加大了对民间意识形态、宗教信仰自由的打击力度，各地政府管理部门亦对基督教等不同宗教信仰群体及其聚会点采取了更激烈的打压逼迫，在此前提下，其所在教会尽管因加入“三自教会”已被官方认可，同时历时<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年，信徒达<span lang="EN-US">500</span>多人，但是仍被地方当局作为整治对象，遭到恶意打压与惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名教会负责者即骨干成员被辽阳市太子河区警方突然统一刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被辽阳市太子河区检察院以涉“非法经营罪”正式批捕，指控其身为教会负责人，自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，违反国家相关规定，唆使其教会骨干成员以“基督教朝光教会”名义购进、卖出海外非法宗教出版物<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万余本，涉及金额<span lang="EN-US">49</span>万多元，属于非法买卖行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院一审以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李芳兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西省南昌市进贤县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。因修炼法轮功遭多次迫害关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，李芳兰因父亲去世，从青海西宁儿子家里回老家奔丧，在西宁火车站进站过安检时被搜包，包里带有大法的书籍和手机，西宁火车站派出所抓捕了李芳兰，借口是扰乱社会治安秩序。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年正月初<span lang="EN-US">9</span>她被关押到江西省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/8/451659.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/8/451659.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁沈阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共镇压法轮功，李凤芝因坚持信仰遭拘留、劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被皇姑区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，因被迫害的双眼无视力被保外就医。王金凤和李凤芝于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被皇姑区黄河派出所、皇姑区国保警察抓捕构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，沈阳市两位善良妇女王金凤、李凤芝坚持修炼法轮大法真、善、忍，被于洪区法院判刑：王金凤<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李凤芝<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚金五千元。李凤芝刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/4/450397.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李钢：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。李钢老人<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月生，两年前，老人曾被绑架，被非法批捕，但因身体亮起红灯，被非法关押在看守所<span lang="EN-US">80</span>天后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚回家。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭绑架、构陷，大连市沙河口区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李广清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北云梦县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>出生，家住云梦县邱聂大队。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日晚上，李广清在云梦县黄香大道与建设东路交汇处给路人赠送法轮功法轮功资料时，被<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个穿黑衣服的警察抓捕到云梦县城关水陆派出所，随后被刑事拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日湖北省孝感市安陆市法院对李广清进行走过场式的庭审后，对李广清判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/9/%E6%B9%96%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%91%E6%A2%A6%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E5%B9%BF%E6%B8%85%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441090.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李桂华（黑龙江）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，佳木斯市木材厂退休工人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日下午三点多钟，李桂华在黑龙江省佳木斯市通江街与维新路交叉口处，李桂华给一名五十岁左右的男士讲法轮功真相时，遭报警，后被抓捕，被送到佳木斯市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李桂华被佳木斯市向阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李桂华不服上诉到佳木斯市中级法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，佳木斯市中级法院裁定维持向阳区法院对李桂华的一审原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李桂华（山东）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东聊城市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁左右。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，济南市铁路公安局、聊城市火车站派出所联合聊城市东昌府区国保大队、古楼派出所共十几个警察，闯入聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员华丽琴家中，把陈军、华丽琴、孙秀娥、李桂华、张亮、徐绍霞（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）和华丽琴的丈夫共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人，抓捕到火车站派出所。火车站派出所对每位学员采指纹、勒索每人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元保证金，同时在当晚和第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天分别对<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位法轮功学员及郭秀萍等抄家，抢走了大法书、真相资料和个人财物。第二天后取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又遭抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被刑事拘留、关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李国庆刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">安徽省阜阳市临泉县法轮功学员。王翠兰、王翠萍、王兰英、李海涛等人，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日送往安徽省宿州监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年修炼法轮功。为宣传法轮功真相，李海艳利用回家乡探访亲友的机会，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，在通海县城东苑小区散发法轮功真相资料，被通海县公安局抓捕，并被通海县法院以莫须有的罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；在县公安局、看守所及监狱关押期间遭到铐重镣、双手反铐、不让睡觉、强行抽血、打骂和欺凌被迫害得全身浮肿，不能站立及正常行走。唐玉、李海艳两女士<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，在昆明市西山区卢家新村路边向路人散发法轮功宣传品，后被抓捕。当局指控两位善良女士犯了所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被昆明市西山区法院视频开庭，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下达判决书（<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>）云<span lang="EN-US">0112</span>刑初<span lang="EN-US">758</span>号，唐玉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月、罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；李海艳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元。李海艳</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑期至：<span href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/25/446758.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李洪财：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省平度市人，平度市古岘镇山头村居民，青岛市即墨市大信镇“福顺废旧物品回收站”经营者，维权访民。李延香的丈夫。其妻子李延香因维权被山东平度市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，刑满释放；其妻子在出狱后因其夫妇二人继续维权抗争，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，夫妻二人都被平度市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘、逮捕。目前李延香被羁押于青岛市第二看守所，丈夫李洪财被羁押于青岛市过渡性看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被大兴区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span Roman&quot;;">李怀庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆民营企业家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名员工均已离职）。随后，警察冻结了其公司和个人的近亿元资产。家属和律师收到的李怀庆的罪名先是“涉黑”，现在又改成“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，家属和律师原本已经收到了重庆市中级人民法院在这一天开庭审理李怀庆案件的通知，可诡异的是，家属和律师很快又收到一纸延期审理的通知书。这一延期，延到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月还音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在重庆开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，李怀庆被庆市第一中级法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法拘禁罪四项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。李怀庆是于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被警方以涉黑名义抓捕，其名下资产同时被全部冻结。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日家属收到重庆市南川监狱的信件，告知李怀庆已转到该监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span 0pt;">天津市河北区法轮功学员。李慧和郑庆兰<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因讲法轮功真相被抓捕，李慧、郑庆兰被关押在天津河北区看守所。近一年于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">12</span>月被重庆石桥铺高新区公安分局抓捕，被劳教两年，关押在重庆茅家山女子劳教所。。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年生。云南宣威市龙场镇浓场村人，在昆明打工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，法轮功学员杨靖波、武存仙、倪会仙由于在小区粘贴「法轮大法好！真善忍好！」不干胶，和向住户赠送「天赐洪福」法轮功小册子，被安宁市金方街道办事处不法人员告发，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被安宁市国保警察抓捕。在抓捕杨靖波时，不法警察抓捕了在杨靖波家的法轮功学员李家周，并且进行抄家；又到李家周家里抢走了笔记本计算机、打印机及真相数据。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州中山大学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，广西横县人，大学毕业，住中山大学南校园西北区。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因去北京上访，她曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，关押到广州市槎头女子劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月在家被海珠区公安分局及新港街派出所警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/5/451530.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李建新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠州市人，人称“惠州区伯”， 实名举报人。因长期网上实名举报广东惠州官员的贪腐行为，引起媒体关注和社会热议。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因其举报惠州市副市长黄锦辉，随遭遇报复性砍伤并被泼硫酸，导致其一只眼睛失明、手脚被砍断，留下终身残疾。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因其继续维权，坚持网络实名举报，被惠州市惠城区警方以涉“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被惠阳区检察院以涉“敲诈勒索”和“非法占用耕地”二罪批捕，并被羁押于惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被起诉于惠州市惠阳区法院，后其案又被因故移交到惠州市惠东县检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，河南太康县法轮功学员，本来是太康县回族小学教师。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功遭无端打压以后，因坚持信仰而屡遭迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，李杰和法轮功学员李慧平、谷玉荣、李艳华等人到乡下散发法轮功资料，被太康逊母口镇派出所抓捕，分别关押，李杰被关押在太康看守所，李慧平等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被关押在周口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李杰判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾基督教圣约家园教会传道。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日晚七点，临汾圣约家园教会<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余人在外举办亲子营活动，被近<span lang="EN-US">170</span>位警察冲击，当场控制同工李洁、韩晓栋，其他人员没收手机，全部被要求给开机密码，搜身，连夜带回临汾，并被等候在尧庙特警大队门口全临汾市所有派出所警察带走。警方在同工李洁、韩晓栋同工家搜查带走一些书籍资料。后李洁及其妻子李珊珊、韩晓栋被指定居所监视居住。李洁于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因被控涉嫌“诈骗罪”被临汾市公安局刑事拘留，被羁押在山西省临汾市尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_4.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_4.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李金兰：广东</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">省肇庆市端州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，广东省肇庆市封开县人，家住肇庆市端州区。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月李金兰开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，她被封开县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，在广东省女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被端州区公安分局警察抓捕，关押到端州区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被德庆县法院<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年</span>，罚金一万元。李金兰上诉后，肇庆市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450331.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450331.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李晶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，李晶女士被长春市经开区分局与深圳街派出所警察抓捕并抢走她家的房门钥匙，警方后到出租屋抄家，抄走惠普高速打印机四台、激光打印机一台、电脑笔记本一台，真相电话十六部、大法书籍两套、大法真相资料等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在经开区法院被庭审，庭审没有通知李晶家属。目前李晶仍被非法关押在长春第四看守所，现在身体出现腹部疼痛，流血现象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日得知李晶被判刑十年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李军才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省新乡市原阳县基督教牧师。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">近年来，因反对中共当局强拆十字架，拒绝把教堂内“爱神爱人”标语改成“爱国爱教”及在教堂内建国旗台，随遭河南省当局打压逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被新乡市原阳县警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑事拘留，另有三名教会同工（即神职工作人员）亦被抓捕，随后几日，其所在中心堂十字架迅速被当地宗教局、公安局及城管等多个部门联合强拆，教堂内“爱神爱人”等标语被清除，教堂内被强行竖立起五星红旗；一个多月后，被抓三名同工均获取保候审，而其却被一直羁押不放，后被原阳县检察院正式批捕，指控其涉嫌“职务侵占、妨害公务和销毁账目”；截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件已在两度退回公安局补充侦查后，再次移送检察院，进入审查起诉阶段；据悉，其儿子称，当局对其父亲的一切指控均属莫须有罪名，旨在对其拒绝与官方合作态度进行刻意“打击报复”。在被关押长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个多月后，河南新乡原阳县家庭教会牧师李军才于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被以“职务侵占”、“妨害公务”及“销毁账目”三罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。另三人均判缓刑。目前被羁押于新乡市原阳县看守所（河南省新乡市原阳县葛埠口乡丘庙村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">453500</span>。）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李俊华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。李俊华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李柯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉籍，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日生，汉族，大学学历，被捕前无业。李柯于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日从武汉乘火车前往西宁，途中换上藏袍，于次日前往塔尔寺，在下午<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点<span lang="EN-US">04</span>分购票进入寺院。并且在塔尔寺不同的地方展示标语和雪山狮子旗和<span lang="EN-US">FREE TIBET(</span>自由西藏<span lang="EN-US">)</span>标语，，让路过游客帮忙拍照。随后被塔尔寺驻寺警察拘留，随后于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被正式批捕。该案于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在西宁市中级人民法院审理，李柯被控煽动分裂国家罪，当庭没有宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李兰强：北</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">京房山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。毕业于北京师范大学，曾在北京市海淀区太平路中学任数学教师。一九九七年十月，李兰强开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，李兰强被中共绑架，非法关押在看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱迫害。曾经二次被劳教迫害共四年、被判刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日晚，李兰强在发放法轮功资料时被人举报，遭西潞派出所警察抓捕，被关押在房山看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月遭房山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。随后李国庆、女儿李蕾被关押在芦台派出所；妻子于波被刑拘。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李蕾刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><b mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李立鑫等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括李立鑫在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。李立鑫被判刑五年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" 0pt;">李力壮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年毕业于哈尔滨医科大学，。他曾是哈尔滨医科大学附属第一医院骨外科主治医生。曾因坚持信仰和平上访，遭多次关押、抄家，两次劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑，经受了各种酷刑折磨，精神、肉体遭受了巨大的创痛，有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半是在囚禁中度过的。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：李力壮被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，李林已被开庭，当庭被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</b>此次是李林第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被判刑，此前两次李林曾被判刑合计有<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b>：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李玲莲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东省梅州市梅城法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚款三万五千元。后上诉，二审维持原判，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劫持到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李美莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员。自一九九九年七月，法轮功遭受江氏中共集团镇压以来，李美莲为坚持自己的信仰，告诉世人法轮功被迫害的真相，曾遭两次劳教（共计约三年多）、一次判刑（五年）。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李美莲再次被抓捕，李美莲在江西省女子监狱脚筋被割断致残，丈夫离世，家中的儿子无人照看，生意兴旺的店铺无人料理关闭，父母双亲中有一个永远地离开了她。目前获悉其已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李麦英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东潍坊坊子区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁。山东潍坊坊子区教育局退休职工。她因坚持信仰，被多次劳教、关押洗脑迫害，多年被剥夺工作权利，工资也被<span lang="EN-US">610</span>截留。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底，李麦英被区国保劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，李麦英再次被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，李麦英因张贴大法好不干胶，被摄像头录影，遭到凤凰派出所警察抓捕。家中被查抄，后来被“取保候审”回家，坊子区国保大队已经对她起诉了，据说“案子”已经走到法院阶段。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，潍坊市坊子区法院人员，到坊子区教育局退休职工李麦英家，通知她要对她开庭。李麦英表示自己无罪，不会到庭。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，山东省潍坊市坊子区国保，强行将李麦英抓捕，把她劫持到坊子区法院开庭，判刑她<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现在李麦英被羁押在何处还未知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/1/450288.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬，黄坤益、李美荣夫妇去单县黄冈镇发放法轮功小册子时被镇派出所警察抓捕。李美荣老人被送到菏泽市女子看守所关押，黄坤益老人因高血压被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被通过视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，李美荣老人<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，黄坤益老人<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E8%8F%8F%E6%B3%BD%E5%B8%82%E5%8D%95%E5%8E%BF%E9%BB%84%E5%9D%A4%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E7%BE%8E%E8%8D%A3%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430285.html"><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李敏舫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，宝鸡消防厂退休职工，家住宝鸡市金台区宝平路。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日以取保候审的方式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，宝鸡市金台区检察院通知李敏舫已被转为监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省襄阳市谷城县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共当局开始迫害法轮功后，李明曾经遭受<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被再次被抓捕、构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，他目前仍被关押在湖北沙洋范家台监狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>监区，每天被迫从事奴工劳作。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445761.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445761.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李培高：云</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1935</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁。男，云南建工安装股份有限公司高级工程师，<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年退休，独居在家。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月李培高开始修炼法轮功。李培高自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年“<span lang="EN-US">720</span>”中共江泽民集团开始迫害法轮功以来，遭十多次抓捕、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次抄家、两次被判刑共<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，李培高发放法轮功资料被西山区公安局国保大队抓捕、抄家，因血压高而“取保候审”，随后遭到西山区法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，监外执行。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，李培高发法轮功日历时被昆明市金碧路派出所警察抓捕，李培高于当晚回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，已经<span lang="EN-US">83</span>岁的李培高再次被警察抓捕后。西山区永昌派出所警察电话通知李培高的家人，说李培高已被关进云南省第一监狱，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月后才能探视。长时间以来，监狱以疫情为由拒绝探视，目前已经<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁的李培高身心状况如何，令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/6/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E86%E5%B2%81%E9%AB%98%E7%BA%A7%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E6%9D%8E%E5%9F%B9%E9%AB%98%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-434429.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">昆明市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，黑龙江人。曾因修炼法轮功被判刑两年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，法轮功学员张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。李萍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E8%90%8D%E3%80%81%E7%94%B0%E4%BA%91%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441414.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李其文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东临清市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日左右被临清国保抓捕，被非关押于临清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日李其文被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李谦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住昆明市西山区白马干休所。因坚持修炼法轮功，李谦女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早上，因疑似派出所警察对她进行跟踪和监控，李谦只身来到昆明市棕树营派出所反映情况，并讲述法轮功被迫害真相，警察在送她出来的时候，李谦给了她几份法轮功真相资料，并嘱咐她退出邪党（党、团、队）组织才能保平安。结果被派出所警察抓捕抄家。关押在昆明市看守所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日李谦即被昆明市西山区公安分局逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被昆明市西山区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金一万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被送到云南省第二女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李翘楚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生，女权主义者，劳工问题研究者。大学本科毕业于中国人民大学劳动人事学院，研究生毕业于英国约克大学并获公共政策硕士学位，其后于清华大学从事研究助理的工作。李翘楚长期参与、关注和研究中国大陆的劳工、女权和民间维权议题。她的研究领域涉及劳工视角的养老保险等政策问题。此外，她还积极参加各种民间自发行动，比如声援北京郊区“清理低端人口”事件中的农民工、反<span lang="EN-US">996</span>、<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>、武汉疫情下的性别暴力问题等。<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>公民案发生后，当局大规模搜捕参与厦门聚会的公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，李翘楚在她的男友许志永流亡期间被北京警方传唤<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时，她之后在网络发表《戴手铐跨新年：<span lang="EN-US">12</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">∙</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被传唤经过》，由此开始实名发声，声援<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>案。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李翘楚被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被指定居所监视居住<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个。她根据自己被秘密关押的经历写下了《李翘楚：被连坐煽颠、指定监视居住的<span lang="EN-US">120</span>天》系列文章，详细讲述了自己被关押期间所遭受的酷刑及不人道虐待。当李翘楚了解到许志永在指监期间遭受酷刑后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日就伙食问题向临沂市公安局寄出了政府信息公开申请，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日就伙食远低于国家标准和高价买餐的问题对临沭县看守所进行了控告，就驻看守所检察官的不履行监督职责进行了投诉，并对临沂市公安局局长和临沂县看守所所长的违法行为进行控告。<span lang="EN-US"> 2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李翘楚被山东警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”押往临沂，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李翘楚案被退回临沂市公安局补充侦查，期限一个月。而此前李翘楚家属申请的取保候审被驳回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日代理律师会见了李翘楚，翘楚狱中病情加重。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">家属申请取保候审再次被口头拒绝。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，律师第<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次视频会见李翘楚。得知李翘楚在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日两次外提到临沂市第四人民医院就诊，医生增加了治疗幻听的药物，服用后她的幻听症状有所缓解。但不系统的治疗，导致了翘楚月经闭经，虚胖等严重副作用。李翘楚母亲特别担忧翘楚的身体和精神状况，已第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>次申请取保候审，此前全部申请均被拒绝。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前李翘楚被关押在临沂市看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">）<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李翘楚代理律师收到临沂市人民检察院于今年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日提交至中级人民法院的起诉书。起诉书列出李翘楚数条“罪证”：与许志永系恋人关系，为许搭建个人博客，宣扬颠覆国家政权思想，并以此认定李翘楚煽动颠覆国家政权、推翻社会主义制度，其行为应以煽动颠覆国家政权罪追究其刑事责任。此前，李翘楚幻听的症状加剧，伴随意识模糊，精神恍惚，家人申请对其取保候审均遭拒绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_36.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/7-10.html"><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李峭松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，广东化州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。自中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功以来，李峭松因坚持讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，多次被抓捕，在劳教所、洗脑班、监狱被关押迫害，累计达<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，李峭松在天河区棠下金棠苑小区给民众派送法轮功资料，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，他在家中，被天河区公安分局国保和棠下派出所警察抓捕，被关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，李峭松被天河区检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被构陷到海珠区检察院，十月份，被构陷到海珠区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年秋，李峭松被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。他提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a
