mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎金凤<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省云浮市法轮功学员。黎金凤于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被云安区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份上诉维持原判，将在广州女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432491.html#211012222131-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432491.html#211012222131-2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎容好：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省中山市小榄镇维权人士。黎容好是因为一家九口人，被地方官员以其婆婆是再婚女为由，剥夺了集体经济组织成员身份，成为了中国特色的“空挂户”，失去了生产与生存（承包地、生产劳动，股份分配，宅基地）等权利。在黎容好上访维权中，一直默默地帮助那些比自己更艰难的访民，在北京有访民形象大使之美誉，也无数次遭到包括被构陷判刑等残酷迫害。在中共十九届六中全会前夕，广东当局雇佣地痞流氓，每天<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时对黎容好实施跟踪、盯梢等维稳。为了常年上访维权的黎容好老了有个基本保障，黎容好的兄弟姐妹凑钱为其购买了社会保险，不料在冤案后被人社局给停发了，完全靠家人帮助生活。黎容好在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日和家人一起，去广州看望朋友，随后被抓被带回中山市，可能是她近一段时间关注了正在狱中绝食抗争的公民记者张展的安危。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，黎容好女士的家人收到公安的刑事拘留通知书，称黎容好因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪被刑事拘留，现羁押在中山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_64.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_64.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黎芸：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">成都市新都区法轮功学员，女士，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁。因坚持修炼法轮功，被中共当局多次关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日黎芸被成都市公安局新都区分局桂湖派出所抓捕，关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多；后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被成都市新都区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447879.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447879.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎智英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1948</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Jimmy Lai Chee-ying</span>，生于中国广州市，祖籍广东省顺德市，现为香港永久性居民，佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>）集团公司老板，香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒及《壹周刊》创办人，香港知名商人，香港民主派政党及组织的重要资助者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年，曾因生活穷困而被迫随广东发生的大规模“逃港潮”，借道澳门逃亡香港谋生，后经努力拼搏，于<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年创办了连锁服装品牌佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>），并迅速使之成为当时风靡中港台的主要时装品牌之一；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因同情天安门民主运动中的抗议学生，其旗下的佐丹奴印制了大量印有民运口号的<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤供人们游行抗议时穿着，其本人也发表公开信敦促时任中国总理的李鹏下台谢罪，遂遭到六四镇压之后北京对香港商人的首批整肃，佐丹奴集团公司在中国大陆的全部业务被当局封杀，致其公司损失惨重，被迫低价出售股权；自此，其弃商从文，转而投身传媒事业，先后创办了壹传媒、《壹周刊》和《苹果日报》，但又因时常抨击中共时弊而被中国大陆禁止入境，其经手的报刊书籍亦被列入黑名单；长期以来，曾因其是香港民主运动（如香港雨伞运动、香港“反送中”抗议活动等）的重要支持者和资助商，故备受北京当局及香港建制派的批评、斥责，甚至指控其捐款为黑金；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因与美国副总统彭斯及美国国务卿蓬佩奥委会面，谈及香港现状及未来前途等事宜，而遭到中共当局的极度仇视和要打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被香港警方以涉嫌“非法集结罪”抓捕，后被释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被以触犯香港《国安法》，涉嫌“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”及“串谋欺诈及煽动罪”拘捕，后暂获保释；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又被指控“欺诈罪”而收监逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天后，再被加控“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”被庭审；后其虽暂获保释，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日再度被捕，关押于香港荔枝角收押所，后与同案民主派高层领袖李卓人被香港西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8.18</span>维园“六四集会案”及<span lang="EN-US">8.31</span>“港岛游行案”进行宣判，其二人同时被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；之后很快其持有的壹传媒公司股份（市值超过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>亿元港币）及对其他三家公司在香港银行账户内所拥有的财产均被香港国安局冻结；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又被香港西九龙法院就其<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“港岛游行案”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四集会案”数次庭审宣判，刑期共计<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，再被以其名下的力高公司涉嫌违反与特区政府香港科技园公司订立的地契为由，被特区高等法院以“欺诈罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">200</span>万港元（<span lang="EN-US">25.69</span>万美元<span lang="EN-US">/179</span>万元人民币），取消担任公司董事资格<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；另有“勾结外国势力危害国家安全罪”案将推迟<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）再审。目前在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/59.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/59.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉长年：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安丰盛基督教教会牧师。自从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日西安市十里铺派出所以“诈骗罪”为由将西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师带走，现已被执行指定居所监视居住，另外一位教会的同工廉旭亮，也以同一罪名被执行指定居所监视居住。还有一位教会会友付娟也被密押一直未放，罪名尚不明悉。目前三人均被关押在政府指定的某个地方。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉旭亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安丰盛基督教教会同工。自从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日西安市十里铺派出所以“诈骗罪”为由将西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师带走，现已被执行指定居所监视居住，另外一位教会的同工廉旭亮，也以同一罪名被执行指定居所监视居住。还有一位教会会友付娟也被密押一直未放，罪名尚不明悉。目前三人均被关押在政府指定的某个地方。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/6.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">练日光：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省惠州市博罗县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住阳春市春城镇<span lang="EN-US">9</span>头坡村。练日光<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年毕业于阳江师范学院，毕业后在阳春市春湾镇卫国乡小学教书，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年调到合水镇平北小学，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年调到营讯小学。因为修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他被阳春市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到阳江监狱迫害，随后他被开除公职。从监狱黑窝出来后，阳春市公安局将他列入管控对象，合水镇综治信访维稳中心对他长期监控和骚扰。练日光在灵泉学堂教数学。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>时左右，博罗县公安局国保大队几乎倾巢出动，和九潭派出所警察一块，以查经营为由，从邻居家闯入灵泉学堂，查抄。查抄中，发现有法轮功书籍，警察将赵天华抓捕，他的妻子蔡惠斌、灵泉学堂的教师陈华良、练日光一起被抓捕，被关押到博罗县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被惠州市惠城区法院判决：练日光被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁春华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林市龙潭区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在吉林市大华市场与商家兑换真相币时，被警察跟踪绑架，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元左右真相币被警察抢走，梁春华先被行政拘留十天。三月二十七日拘留到期，警察直接将梁春华拉走，抄家，抢走工资卡、存折等物品，家里被劫的空荡荡。然后将梁春华又劫持到吉林市看守所关押，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被关押在吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁顺景<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，广东省梅州市梅县区城东镇人，原中国工商银行梅州分行职工，梅州城区江南团结路苏泊尔电器店负责人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因为人谦和、厚道而深受他人好评；又因其与其妻邓秀芬在当地共同承办苏泊尔电器店（主营电器厨器专卖批发），生意上注重诚实守信，随其公司至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底时已有较大发展；但因梁顺景、邓秀芬夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在信仰追求上笃信并积极宣传法轮功，随遭广东省梅州市当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在开车外出讲解宣传法轮功时，被事先蹲坑等候的梅州市梅江区警方及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室人员联合抓走，其家遭查抄，当场搜走法轮功书籍多套、计算机、打印机及银行卡、身份证等个人对象（如）多件，并将其日用汽车也拉走扣留；次日，其妻因血压高达<span lang="EN-US">180/230</span>，让家人暂时接回，其本人则被梅江区警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，关押至梅江区芹黄看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被梅江区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在梅州市梅江区法院开庭审理；虽因该法院违反法定诉讼程序，其辩护律师曾据理要求法院重新开庭审判，但其与其妻仍然被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判；其中<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">，梁顺景被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，其妻邓秀芬被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并各处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，经广东省梅州市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其妻邓秀芬刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所时被查出身体长有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个肿瘤，在被庭审时其辩护权及辩护律师执业权被剥夺；其承办的苏泊尔电器店因长时无人经营，故被迫关门。目前在广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱（广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘镇<span lang="EN-US">/</span>广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">梁琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</b>其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。梁琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市丰台区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，梁新在北京东城区亮果厂胡同发法轮功资料时，被监控器监控；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，梁新被东城区石景山派出所抓捕、抄家，许多私人物品被抢劫。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，梁新被北京东城区公安分局非法拘留。关押在北京市东城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁耀敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，山东海阳市法轮功学员。其原本是海阳市公安局刑警队痕迹检验工程师，技术精湛，经她鉴定破获了许多大案、要案，是全省少有的女性侦察技术人员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共江开始疯狂迫害法轮功，梁耀敏仅仅因为坚持自己的信仰、继续修炼法轮功，经历了被关押、开除公职、关洗脑班、关精神病院、劳教、判刑、停发退休金等种种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在山东省女子监狱遭受关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，山东海阳市国保警察共抓捕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员：梁耀敏、张俊峰、张吉国、王成刚、纪力骁、隋伟丽、于海勇和王雪梅夫妻。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，梁耀敏与另外几位女法轮功学员被关押到烟台牟平看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，梁耀敏被批捕，同时由烟台牟平看守所转押到烟台福山看守所。年逾<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁的法轮功学员梁耀敏，被抓捕、关押在烟台市看守所，由于长期的被关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在被海阳市（凤城）法院的视频庭审期间，当庭出现严重的心绞痛情况，生命垂危，看守所怕出事当场实施紧急抢救。梁耀敏<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被开庭，公诉方捏造伪证的行径再次被曝光。辩护律师依法逐条说明了公诉方提供的各项所谓人证、物证均无法律效力，要求当庭释放。但是最终梁耀敏被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html"><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁展鸿</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东深圳市福田区法轮功学员，女士，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，梁展鸿老人在家中被抓捕，所谓的原因是她给小区保安讲法轮功被举报。遭受绑架几个月后，梁展鸿老人从福田看守所转入南山看守所，目前已经被非法关押在南山看守所将近一年。后得知已遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，未上诉。目前已收到通知，将被送广州女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁子亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人，梁子亮与妻子李银秀，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廖小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省梅州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年，她开始修炼法轮功。因持续宣传法轮功，曾遭劳教、拘留。因发真相资料被监控查到，廖小平<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日上午被当地五洲派出所抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被梅州市梅县区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，罚款一万五千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/25/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%BB%96%E5%B0%8F%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440476.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/25/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E6%A2%85%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%BB%96%E5%B0%8F%E5%B9%B3%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440476.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林春芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，湖北省丹江口市人，原丹江口市丁家营镇丁营大道<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号村民、丹江口市南水北调中线工程库区农村移民，现北京市海淀区黄庄小区<span lang="EN-US">813</span>楼<span lang="EN-US">312</span>室居民，基督徒，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。早年，曾因是湖北省丹江口市南水北调中线工程库区的农村移民，理应得到的政府占地补偿款一直未能得到，随向村镇等各级管理部门“反映问题”，自此屡遭打压；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因自家房屋面临强拆，其及与其同住的父母在拒强拆中遭殴打，情急之下 ，其用汽油欲自焚以示抗议；事后其虽赶到当地警局报案，但竟了无结果，当局依然不予公正、恰当解决；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因上访而被丹江口市丁家营镇警方刑拘，并被关进丹江口市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，又被丹江口市警方以“扰乱单位秩序”、“阻碍执行职务”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，再被当地警方关进黑监狱，且其房屋被夷为平地，屋内贵重物品均丢失，财产、财务及家畜等尽遭掩埋和损坏；后其因此继续上访，并到北京寻求信访帮助，不料遭到更多的侮辱欺凌、拘押和关黑监狱等迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因住京维权遭截访，先被关在丹江口市驻京办招待所，后又被秘押至丹江口市文华宾馆<span lang="EN-US">103</span>房间，并被强行脱光衣服搜身，致其倍感羞辱，曾为此绝食抗议<span lang="EN-US">7</span>昼夜；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被更换地址持续秘关<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，期间遭十几名看守其的黑社会性质的男性青年多次殴打和虐待，致其因痛不欲生，拔下窗户上的钉子割腕自杀；后幸免遇难，但仍被当局强逼写材料，不写就打；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其被迫在丁家营镇政府提供的协议书上签字画押，并写下不再上访保证书，才终得获释返家；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因在京上访期间，受到北京基督教圣爱团契家庭教会对其生活及信仰上的帮助与支持，随与教会信徒们一起学习《圣经》，并于次年受洗而成为一名基督徒；之后，其信访要求有所解决，地方政府为其及父母修盖了房子，作为其在水库移民中的经济补偿（当然还有土地等其他问题并未解决），而其此时也在北京结婚，其丈夫因是北京公民并在北京工作当医生，随其成为名副其实的北京媳妇，并与丈夫长居京城。之后，因其原籍住宅的户主名字，在当年登记的是其父母之名而非其本人，随其在父母明确授意的前提下，多次向有关部门提出申请，要求将户主姓名更为自己的姓名，然而相关政府部门却对其申请久拖未予解决，其随被迫再次在京信访投诉；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被丹江口市警方以“寻衅滋事”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被原籍截访人员突然带走，遣回原籍后被丹江口市十堰市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并被关押在十堰市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被丹江口市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，追溯其曾于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来一直因房屋拆迁问题在国家非信访部门上访，此行为已与现行相关法律规条相抵触，又加之中共十•一<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年党庆将至，为防止其再度维权上访，给党庆造成不良影响，故而被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被湖北省丹江口市法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。目前在湖北省武汉女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">(</span>湖北省武汉市乔口区宝丰一路<span lang="EN-US">97</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">430030)</span>服刑。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/4_19.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/4_19.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林大卫：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，祖籍不详，美籍华人，英文名<span lang="EN-US">David Lin</span>，美国爱荷华州（<span lang="EN-US">Iowa</span>）和加利福尼亚州（<span lang="EN-US">California</span>）经济顾问，基督徒，美国基督复临安息日会牧师，针对中国家庭教会的宣道士，中国在押良心犯。自移民美国以来，早期曾专注于养家糊口，并自己熟知的领域一直努力工作；后入籍成为美国公民，曾在爱荷华州和加利福尼亚州担任政府官员的经济顾问；来美之初，其并无基督信仰，并认为只有无知的人才会信教，但多年之后，当其妻子成为基督徒后，其开始深入了解基督教信仰；后其受洗成为基督徒，并自此开始积极参与教会的服事活动；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，因其经常到中国旅行，期间深刻感受到基督教福音在中国广传的必要性，遂立定心志，以期能从中国官方最终获得开始基督教事工的许可；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，已是教会牧师的他开始了中国大陆差传宣道之旅；此期间，因中国政府为成功申办<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年奥运会，曾一度营造“外松”形象，故而一时吸引了众多基督教工作者来华倡导，但实因中共本质上的思想意识倾向与基督教宣传的价值取向完全相左，遂在<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年前后启动的一项代号为“台风五号”秘密行动中，数以百计的外国来华传教士被驱逐；其亦在此打压行动中，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，因帮助中国家庭教会盖一座教堂而被中国警方突然拘押和被禁止离境；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，其被中国某检察院以涉嫌“合同诈骗罪”予以批捕，指控其因“合同欺诈”而触犯了中国相关法律，故而应予逮捕、重判；随后其案很快被检察院起诉，并将其案宗移交至中国某法院审查；同年，终被中国某法院以“合同诈骗罪”枉法重判无期徒刑；据悉，被判之初，其家人尚选择保持沉默和低调处事，因其表明已将监狱视为施教、分享信仰和鼓励来自<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多个国家的囚犯的机会，故其在狱中建立了每周一次的礼拜天祷告会，并致力于将圣经译成中文；但时至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2019</span>年初，其在与家人的定期电话中突然明确要求帮助其尽早获得释放；后从官方得知其健康状况正在恶化，疑指可能“遭非人道虐待”等，遂开始寻求美国拜登总统及政府的帮助，以期能被无罪释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉，其已被中共当局执行减刑，但刑期仍需至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前服刑监狱不详。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/david-lin_15.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/david-lin_15.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林闺臣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：福州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，系福建省农科院耕作所退休女职工。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在发法轮功资料时，被福州市公安局鼓楼区温泉派出所警察抓捕到明清县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被批捕。马尾区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月对她庭审，后对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林国兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省通化市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，家住吉林省通化市东昌区。自<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年林国兰开始修炼法轮功以来，受益良多。林国兰<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日去通化县江沿等地发放法轮功资料，被通化县公安局国保大队警察抓捕、构陷，后悉已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初被送进吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/27/450144.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/27/450144.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林乐宏：女，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，大学本科毕业，家住深圳市南山区。林乐宏和马彦平都暂在深圳龙岗区布吉镇大芬油画村租住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上，林乐宏、马彦平在大芬油画村租住房内，被龙岗区公安分局国保及布吉派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，两人被关押到龙岗区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，警察再次对<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人的租住房进行了查抄，将法轮功书籍、资料、电脑、打印机、塑封机、切边机、硬盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等个人物品全部劫走。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，林乐宏、马彦平被龙岗区检察院批捕。被关押后，林乐宏多次绝食反迫害，遭看守所强制灌食，健康受到严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，林乐宏被强制灌食后，被送医院所谓“抢救”。从此，林乐宏吃什么吐什么，回到看守所后，身体<span lang="EN-US">1</span>直不好。血压高至<span lang="EN-US">160/180mmHg</span>（低血压高）。她每周需要吸氧<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，只能吃流食，出现心口痛，左手麻木。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，林乐宏、马彦平被盐田区法院庭审。有律师出庭做无罪辩护。为了抵制持续的迫害，从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日始，林乐宏又开始绝食，被连续强制灌食<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天。体重只剩<span lang="EN-US">46</span>公斤，舌根发硬，吞咽困难，胸口时常发闷，血糖极低（不到<span lang="EN-US">3mmol/L</span>），手脚冰凉，特别怕冷，<span lang="EN-US">26</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">︒</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">的气温下还要穿大棉袄。在林乐宏身体健康严重受损的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，盐田区法院宣判，林乐宏被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；马彦平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林久良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">另名林素梁，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">四川</span>成都市新津区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，女，家住成都市新津区<span lang="EN-US">5</span>津街道。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年修炼法轮功。她却因为坚持修炼，遭受中共当局的种种迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被大邑县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。林久良<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午向世人讲法轮功，被成都市大邑县公安局沙渠派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被成都市大邑县法院视频开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446034.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446034.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林茂成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连市金州区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，林茂成给陌生人讲法轮功，被他诬告后遭抓捕抄家，非法拿走大法书籍、计算机、打印机、身份证、驾驶证等物品。林茂成被劫持到派出所期间强制照相，录指纹、声音、验血、做完笔录后，逼他签字未果。半夜后，人被放回，监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，林茂成被大连普兰店检察院批捕，并被大连大孤山边防派出所强制关押在大连开发区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，林茂成被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">是辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林学岁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">浙江省温州市人，基督徒，浙江省温州某归正家庭教会同工，四川省泸州市古蔺县受邀差传倡导者（即受原教会派遣，跨区域给未信者广传福音的基督徒），中国在押良心犯。因笃信耶稣基督，而致力于广传基督教福音并积极参与教会的服事活动，遂深受教会牧者及教友们的喜爱与信任；近年来，因受邀到四川省泸州市古蔺县某一偏远山区看望基督徒，虽欣然前往，但却发现该地区不仅属国家级特困县，而且民众的信仰也甚荒凉，遂决定留在古蔺县，以期用热心、爱心和耐心给未信者传讲福音；然而，自中共当局开始对宗教自由信仰越发严苛的打压之后，其传播基督教活动，如礼拜天聚会、唱赞美诗、查考研读圣经等，引起四川管理者当局的不悦与警戒；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其与另两位基督徒被泸州市古蔺县警方以是“有社会危险性”人员为由，以涉嫌“组织、资助非法聚集罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，另两位基督徒被准予取保候审，但其仍被扣押，并被古蔺县警方以同罪名正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其案被古蔺县警方提交至古蔺县检察院审查起诉；已有律师介入。目前被羁押于四川古蔺县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_68.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_68.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林炎德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九六五年四月出生，家住揭阳市空港区渔湖镇港口村。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，林炎德在使用真相基站发送信息时，被揭阳市公安局空港分局国保和渔湖派出所警察蹲守抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，法院到揭阳市看守所宣判，林炎德被判重刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，他被关押到广东省四会监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林燕梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区水东镇法轮功学员<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b>林燕梅与姐姐林丽珍、外甥吴朝琪（林丽珍的儿子）一家三人<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被茂名市滨海新区公安分局抓捕。林燕梅、林丽珍、吴朝棋在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被电白区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日茂名市茂南区法院主审法官柯学军宣判：林丽珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万；林燕梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金八千；吴朝棋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林在务：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，化名林大海、林忠，福建省福清市人，福清市东瀚镇东瀚村田尾<span lang="EN-US">17</span>号村民，职业不详，“耶和华见证人”信徒、传道人，新疆耶和华见证人教会正规先驱（类似于基督教的长老），中国在押良心犯。因信仰耶和华见证人教派，并被委任在新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒地区做正规先驱（即该教会一种重要职务），在库尔勒市组成家庭聚会，举行上百次大型聚会及成员培训，大力发展信徒，随遭极左思维极强的中共当局严打狠批；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，在“耶和华见证人案”大抓捕中，被库尔勒市警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”与多人悉数抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式逮捕，并被指控称，其因打着基督教旗号，组织教会聚会， “宣扬所谓政治中立，煽动成员及他人不履行公民法定义务”，破坏了国家的法律法规，所以属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人涉邪教案被警方向当地检察院提起公诉；后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被检察院发回补侦，但同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又已被补查重报；至今待审未判，且无更多具体信息；据悉，曾在看守所内因拒绝唱“红歌”等，常遭连体铐、抱铐等体罚虐待。目前被羁押于库尔勒市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘爱华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省辽阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，辽阳市警察跟踪刘爱华。刘爱华被抓捕、抄家，关押在辽阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，刘爱华被灯塔市检察院批捕，后被起诉到灯塔市法院。刘爱华被关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">202</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被灯塔市法院第一次庭审，当日未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点，刘爱华被灯塔市法院第二次开庭后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/2/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432066.html#21101225216-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/2/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432066.html#21101225216-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘伯滨</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年毕业于湖南大学，原为哈尔滨量具刃具厂（国有企业）高级工程师，由于坚持修炼使她受益的法轮大法，曾经被判刑五年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>至<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市、区三十多名法轮功学员被绑架，刘伯滨<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被香坊区警察抓捕、抄家、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日上午刘伯滨被哈尔滨市道里区法院视频远程开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、罚金二万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘嫦娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已年过七旬。刘嫦娥因坚持法轮信仰，多次遭中共迫害，她曾两次被劳教（至少<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年），<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在劳教所、监狱遭到酷刑折磨及劳工奴役。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初在鹰潭市月湖区夏埠乡向民众讲法轮功时被警察抓捕，之后被关押在鹰潭市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被当地中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/14/447633.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘长富</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘长富并抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对刘长富、李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。刘长富刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘长福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林白山市抚松县法轮功学员。刘长福、胡庆兰夫妇在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被抚松县国保伙同新屯子镇派出所警抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午九点左右被靖宇法院远程秘密宣判，刘长福被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，胡庆兰<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。家属未收到任何通知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/22/453424.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/22/453424.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘臣金：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东青岛市崂山区法轮功学员刘臣金、施月英都七十岁左右，家住青岛市崂山区沙子口，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被崂山区公安局警察抓捕，施月英因身体原因第二天回家，被监视居住。刘臣金一直被关押至今。期间，他分别被拘禁于崂山区某处数日及城阳看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年七月底转青岛第一看守所（即墨市普东镇）继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉刘臣金被青岛市市北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/8/444645.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘春爱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员，女，家住北京市西城区阜外地区。刘春爱、李爽、闫勇、岳利永均是北京法轮功学员。李爽在北京一家电子产品公司工作，公司老板是法轮功学员闫勇（闫永）和岳利永夫妇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日刘春爱、李爽、闫勇、岳利永四人均被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月刘春爱、李爽、闫勇、岳利永，经两次开庭后，被判刑——刘春爱、李爽、岳利永，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，分别被罚金四千元，闫勇<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金四千元。目前，他们仍被关押在西城区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/3/452646.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/3/452646.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘春静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，因修炼法轮功，刘春静<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年曾被劳教两年，送佳木斯市西格木劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘春静在发放真相传单时，被人恶意构陷，又遭恶警抓捕被桦南县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押到黑龙江女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在街上递送给人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个护身符卡片，被举报，桦南县胜利派出所警察将刘春静抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘春静<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘春琴</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：湖南省株洲市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原湖南省衡阳轧钢厂职工，一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘春琴多次被绑架、非法关押，在看守所、劳教所、监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被株洲市天元区公安分局泰山路派出所恶警绑架；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被株洲市芦淞区法院秘密非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索罚金五千元；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被送湖南省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘翠梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏石嘴山市惠农区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍在石嘴山市惠农区水城民生片区讲法轮功，贴真相不干胶，被国保大队和园艺派出所便衣警察跟踪抓捕、抄家，当晚三人被放回家。此后，警察便对每位法轮功学员进行暗中监控和跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅等人被国保警察有预谋的抓捕、抄家。刘翠梅是从银川市的家中被警察抓捕到石嘴山市惠农区，在审讯过程中，多次被殴打。当天，余德贞、陈秀萍、史梅兰、刘翠梅被“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，余德贞、史梅兰、陈秀萍、刘翠梅再被抓捕，在石嘴山看守所被关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，余德贞、陈秀萍、史美兰、刘翠梅被石嘴山市大武口区法院判刑。余德贞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金三万元；陈秀萍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金二万五千元；史梅兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，被罚金一万元；刘翠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘达鹏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林榆树市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。原籍吉林省舒兰市人，后搬到榆树市，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因信仰法轮功曾被劳教和判刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，刘达鹏与妻子李春环因在楼下自家车的车筐里发现别人放的真相资料，然后顺便发出去，被人恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，榆树市正阳派出所五个警察闯入刘达鹏、李春环夫妇家中，将二人抓捕。刘达鹏被刑事拘留，妻子李春环被拘留五天。由于疫情，刘达鹏被取保候审一年，他们没被关在拘留所，而是被关押在正阳派出所，两天后，刘达鹏与妻子李春环被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，正阳派出所打电话让刘达鹏和李春环到派出所去一趟，刘达鹏被构陷到德惠市检察院，被批捕，并关押在榆树市看守所。后刘达鹏被德惠法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘德明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏南通维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日一早，无执法权的南通欣宏房屋征收服务有限公司受南通市港闸区住房和建设环境保护局委托，雇佣一批保安拥着挖掘机（犯罪工具），进入南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村，将刘德明的房屋团团围住，并拉上了警戒线，企图强拆，以达到非法圈地的目的。村民们向<span lang="EN-US">110</span>报警。港闸公安分局民警到达现场后，只是谈谈地说了一句：“政府行为，我们管不了”，致使非法圈地的保安更加有恃无恐，对刘德明家围困了整整一夜。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，该公司雇佣的保安用铁锤敲打刘德明的房屋。情势危急，且在民警不作为的情况下，刘德明为捍卫家园才点燃钩机。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，南通市公安局港闸分局以涉嫌故意毁坏财产罪为由，将南通市港闸区永兴街道节制闸村村民刘德明带走调查。次日，该局作出港公（公）拘通字【<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>】<span lang="EN-US">263</span>号拘留通知书，载明对刘德明刑事拘留，现羁押于南通市看守所，并将拘留通知书向刘德明妻子送达。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘富祥</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：重庆维权人士。刘富祥位于重庆市九龙坡区石桥铺正街<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号房屋，因为拆迁问题未与地方政府达成拆迁协议。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，刘富祥和儿子刘汗、侄女刘丽珺、朋友鞠小林在家中休息，被一群不明身份人闯入，将四人打伤打残，刘富祥和儿子刘汗全身多处骨折。随后四人被以妨碍公务罪抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，刘富祥妨碍公务案开庭宣判，到法庭旁听出来的刘富祥的姐姐刘富兰哭诉：弟弟刘富祥被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄儿刘汗被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、侄女刘丽珺被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">22</span>天、鞠小林被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刘富祥刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘刚利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">沈阳市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住沈阳市铁西区。她因传播法轮功，曾经于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被沈河区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在辽宁女子监狱被迫害。狱中遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，她<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年冤狱期满，被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘刚利和女儿去家附近市场买东西时，给民众发放法轮功资料，被沈阳市铁西区公安分局七马路派出所警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被“取保候审”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，刘刚利被七马路派出所抓捕到沈阳市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，刘刚利被沈阳市经济技术开发区检察院批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沈阳经济技术开发区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，家属为刘刚利存钱时发现，看守所存款系统清零，打电话查询得知，刘刚利已经被劫持到辽宁省第二女子监狱，看守所拒绝透露具体投监日期，且无法会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/25/448093.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘广：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。男，职业医生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，警察闯入刘广有家诊所，将法轮功书籍掠走，并将刘广有抓捕关押、刑拘。后移交佳木斯市向阳区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日分别被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘广有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘广友：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">佳木斯桦南县乡村医生，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日生，已七旬。刘广友修炼法轮功二十多年，累计遭关押四次，判刑九年。自<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年仅七年中，他遭迫害勒索及经济损失累计达十三万元左右。刘广友因仗义执言，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月又遭当地警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日他被庭审，遭判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刘广友被桦南县看守所非法关押期间出现脑血栓病状，家属一再要求办保外就医，目前相关单位仍未给他办理。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/23/443963.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 0pt;">刘桂花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省洛阳市洛龙区法轮功学员，女。原家住河南义马市，她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被义马市公安局警察抓捕，被关押在三门峡市看守所至少一年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底洛龙区公安局警察分别抓捕了刘桂花、李晓燕等法轮功学员，把她们关押在洛阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省洛阳市洛龙区法院对法轮功学员刘桂花、李晓燕做出判刑，判刘桂花<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，李晓燕<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刘桂花刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/17/450852.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘国花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省大理州宾川县法轮功学员。一九六八年出生，家住大理州宾川县金牛镇太和农场柳家湾十五队。刘国花曾因向世人赠送神韵晚会光盘遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刘国花于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被抓捕，之后一直被关押在大理州看守所。在家属完全不知情的情况下，就对刘国花开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a
