class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘海康：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江北安市法轮功学员。刘海康于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在家被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘海康的家人才得知刘海康已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现仍被关押在北安市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘红枢</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：又名刘红书，陕西省岐山县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，岐山县京当镇祝家庄社区西戢村营西组人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，刘红枢修炼法轮大法。在法轮大法遭受迫害的最初那几年，刘红枢在新疆打工，在一家出版社工作，在讲法轮功被当地“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”人员绑架、失去了正常工作的机会，被非法劳教。此后经常受到岐山县、祝家庄乡政府人员的骚扰、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日在家里被岐山县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>人员抓捕抄家，关押在岐山县看守所，后来被秘密开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘红霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，女。刘红霞毕业于大连外国语学院俄语专业。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，她因坚持信仰，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被大连市公安局抓捕，被劳动教养，监外执行<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，刘红霞遭大连市西岗区公安分局香工街派出所警察抓捕。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，狱中遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午，刘红霞在楼道里张贴法轮功真相贴时，被跟踪的警察抓捕。刘红霞被关押在大连看守所。自<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，刘红霞开始绝食绝水。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在她身体极度虚弱、半躺在椅子上的情况下，被甘井子区法院强行开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万。刘红霞全程没有发言，律师要求延期开庭的意见被驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，黑龙江密山市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已七旬。因修炼法轮功，刘辉被迫流离失所到鸡西市，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在鸡西被抓捕。她被关押在鸡西看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在被关押在哈尔滨女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/19/453294.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/19/453294.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘会茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，河北省人，知名民营企业家、河北大午农牧集团有限公司前董事长孙大午之妻，河北大午农牧有限公司核心创办人（之一），企业前高层管理者，挂职副监事长，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年起，因承包了一片荒弃的砖窑和坟包地作为投资养殖业，后历经几年发展，随促成与其丈夫孙大午共同创建河北大午农牧集团有限公司之行为，并成为丈夫创业、经营发展以及日后对社会“行公义，好怜悯”等作为的坚实后盾；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，因河北大午农牧集团有限公司孙大午等<span lang="EN-US">25</span>位集团高管及亲属、亲信幕僚等被河北省高碑店市警方悉数带走，并被迅速以涉嫌“寻衅滋事、破坏生产经营罪”指定居所监视居住，其受牵连亦与两个儿媳等分别被带走、刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因其年事已高，又患高血压、糖尿病等多种疾病，且早已不参与大午集团的决策和经营，既不涉及违法犯罪，也不涉及暴力性犯罪，其代理律师随为其先后两次申请变更强制措施（即取保候审），但两次均被警方以“经审查，我局认为刘会茹有可能毁灭、伪造证据、干扰证人作证“为由遭拒；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被高碑店市警方以涉嫌“非法吸收公众存款罪”转正式逮捕；后其案被高碑店市检察院起诉至至高碑店市法院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，终被河北省高碑店市法院一审以“非法吸收公众存款罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同案另两个儿媳及一个侄女被判定罪免罚。目前被羁押于河北省保定市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/3.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘家财</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，湖北省宜昌市人，原宜昌市葛洲坝集团职工，原云南省某工程监理公司工程师，民主维权公民，政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，曾因湖北葛洲坝下岗职工合法权利遭受非法侵害等问题，为了维护数千下岗职工切身利益，积极发起和组建独立工会，领导葛洲坝集团教育经费维权和反腐运动，而被湖北省宜昌市警方逮捕，并于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处管制<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；出狱后，曾前往云南省昭通市谋职，并在某工程监理公司任监理工程师，但工作之余仍坚守民主理念，活跃于网络民主运动其间，为此曾多次遭云南省警方威胁、警告和传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，再次因参与民主维权活动和维权公民发起的“同城饭醉”活动，并在腾讯微博、新浪微博、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>网上转发《李向阳复仇血洗公告（并招募敢死队员）》等，随被当地警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，后又被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”转为刑拘，且关押于湖北省宜昌市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被再次更换罪名以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被湖北省宜昌市中级法院以“煽动颠覆政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，经湖北省高级法院二审裁定，仍被维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，刑满释放。此前在湖北省汉津监狱服刑。据悉，其在狱中常受体罚，尤其是牙齿已严重损坏，不能嚼食物，吃东西靠吞；左颈脖子到左肩到左手均感酸痛，左手大拇指及食指已经麻木；每天腰痛，导致不能正常睡觉；入狱前就患有左心室肥大等心脏病，亟需保外就医，但遭拒。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，有段时间在东莞一个公司做监理。后被宜昌国保要求回到宜昌打工至今。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日早上刘家财跟朋友说他原来的工作单位葛洲坝集团通知他回去处理一个事情，结果被抓了。目前情况不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_34.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_34.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘家玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津静海县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年四十六岁。原静海县市容环卫局干部，静海县静海镇高庄子村人。她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年两次被非法关押在天津大港区板桥女子劳教所，前后五年遭受强制奴役劳动、不让睡觉等迫害，她坚持信仰，不妥协。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年才出狱。刘家玲<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，被关押在天津女子监狱，遭受残忍迫害。刘家玲在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日又失踪，后得知被关押在静海看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获知刘家玲又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘甲兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省蛟河市白石山镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，法轮功学员朱明兰、刘甲兰、山福莲被镇派出所骗去测核酸，录指纹，随后就被关押到吉林市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年二月十九日，吉林省蛟河市白石山镇法轮功学员朱明兰、刘甲兰、山福莲被最终判决，分别为<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前，她们被关押在长春市女子监狱。刘甲兰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/11/444764.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/11/444764.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘建：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，安徽省蚌埠市人，复转军人，安徽省蚌埠市公安局警察，公安部第二批援藏工作组组长，曾荣获西藏自治区公安厅“公安部优秀援藏干部”和“蚌埠市十佳人民警察”荣誉称号，愿蚌埠市警察博物馆筹建办负责人，实名举报人，在押维权人士。早年曾于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年入伍，复原后于<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月参加公安刑警工作；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾参加公安部第二批援藏工作并担任援藏组组长；因其素日工作认真、尽职敬业，故曾先后荣获西藏自治区公安厅“公安部优秀援藏干部”和“蚌埠市十佳人民警察”荣誉称号，并多次被评为省市追逃能手及先进个人、优秀共产党员；近年来，因蚌埠市公安局多次出现私自销毁案件卷宗，导致部分案件变成“无头案”，被害人状告无门，案子始终无法被侦破等黑幕，故其本着良知和职业操守，对蚌埠市公安局（尤指相关负责人及其推卸责任、刑侦不作为和违法乱作为等行为）勇敢的在网上进行了实名举报；然而正因这一举报义举冲闯了当地公安系统相关管理者及其利益集团的私利和名誉，遂遭嫉恨和压制；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，曾因多次网络实名举报而在警局内被十几名公安局领导干部殴打、毁证和不立案，同时局长就站在一旁观看；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因举报称蚌埠市公安局警察“不解决群众提出的问题，却解决提出问题的人”，而被公安局领导叫去谈话，并被威胁要将其“双开”；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，曾目睹在蚌埠市公安局停车场的刷车场内，几名刑警支队同事公然销毁案件的全过程，并用手机进行录像取证，同时呼吁警局分管刑警的局长能站出来对此进行解释，因而遭到现关领导的极端不满和报复性打击；后其举报的问题虽被中央政法委和公安部派出的调查组查实，但却只将部分涉案人员从轻发落，而主要领导毫发无损，自己却身陷囹圄；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因其再次网络实名举报，遂于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被蚌埠市交通分局警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。目前被羁押于蚌埠市看守所（安徽省蚌埠市蚌山区迎宾大道与仁和集高速收费站附近，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">233040</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_99.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_99.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘建新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">福建福州维权人士。福州市仓山区城门镇前锦村村民。刘建新因房屋被强拆近<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，至今无补偿、无安置<span lang="EN-US">.</span>在去年，刘建新因在家被<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时监控，感到非常郁闷，去北京旅游散心，结果遭到维稳人员劫持后被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。因为刘建新在北京既没有信访，更没有违法行为，最后公安只能将其放了。后来，当时的城门镇赵书记就刘建新的诉求组织了一次协调，因为政府不愿意就其违法强拆行为，依法给予安置与赔偿，双方协商未能成功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘建新在北京永定门河边举“冤”字牌，然后跳下去准备了此被官府肆意欺压与压迫的屈辱一生，然后被保安救上来。到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号晩上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，刘建新被送到城门派岀所，关在城门派岀所铁笼里面，其妻子得知消息后赶到，一直等到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号晚上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点之后，派出所告知刘建新被送走了。后获悉其被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被正式批捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘建新从福州市看守所给妻子江国英寄出书信，称当局已对构陷他的所谓寻衅滋事罪一案，在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日进行秘密开庭，公诉机关建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年！其妻子证实，一审仓山区法院没有通知家属旁听。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_85.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_85.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/blog-post_6.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘杰（黑龙江）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江哈尔滨市宾县维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>岁的刘杰，是因为在<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年做生意时，经销的<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余万商品被检察院扣押拒不返回、且销毁案件的案卷材料而上访。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刘杰在北京时，哈尔滨市宾县政府的领导多次给刘杰打电话，说别去国家信访局登记了，回来就给解决问题，还给刘杰买了机票回宾县。当刘杰回宾县后，政法委书记刘宇峰确实组织了听证会，但提出给予<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万困难补助，一次性解决刘杰的诉求，刘杰拒绝了这样的解决方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，刘杰因对由政法委书记刘宇峰组织的听证结果表达不满，被宾县公安局以辱骂了政法委书记刘宇峰为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年“七一”建党百年前夕，宾县公安局曾以刘杰在今年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日到检察院辱骂工作人员为由，又以“寻衅滋事”为由对刘杰拘留<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天。今年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘杰再次去北京上访，在北京拦截了国家信访局大局长李文章的车，被宾县公安局以“寻衅滋事”为由拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。后刘杰的女儿接到辖区派出所电话，告知其父亲已经被刑事拘留，送看守所羁押。刘杰的女儿问自己父亲已经<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁了，之前已两次被行政拘留，是否符合合并为刑事拘留的规定？派出所没有给予回答。据了解，刘杰患有严重高血压、高血压脂、心脏病，且是<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周岁的老人了，已不符合羁押式拘留的规定，现在宾县公安又升级为刑事拘留，看来一心想要维护合法权益的刘老汉是凶多吉少了。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，刘杰又被举报单位宾县检察院正式批捕。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/70.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘金焕</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：广州市番禺区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月出生，毕业于广东省建材中专，原番禺水泥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚上，刘金焕往停在钟村优瑞厂附近的小车门把手上放了几份有关疫情的周报，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，番禺区公安分局国保与钟村派出所出动<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台警车，对刘金焕抓捕抄家，并将刘金焕关押到番禺区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BB%BD%E8%8E%B7%E7%9F%A563%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-434358.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘金萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员。刘金萍于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在家中被警察抓捕、抄家。当地公安、检察院以涉嫌所谓“破坏法律实施”的罪名将她刑事拘留，并将构陷材料递交到向阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日佳木斯市向阳区法院对此开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日向阳区法院对刘金萍判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。收到判决书后，刘金萍委托亲友辩护人上诉。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，佳木斯市中院违反法律程序，剥夺亲友辩护人的权利，没有公开开庭审理就做出了驳回上诉、维持原判的终审裁定。目前刘金萍被关押在佳木斯市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/13/%E4%BD%B3%E6%9C%A8%E6%96%AF%E5%88%98%E9%87%91%E8%90%8D%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%8A%E8%AF%89-%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%A4-441238.html"><b mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘锦明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省兴城市法轮功学员。因在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年控诉江泽民，被构陷到法院，被传唤，没有到庭。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下刘锦明被温泉派出所抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刘锦明现被关押在兴城曹庄看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442549.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘开胜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川泸州市法轮功学员，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年生，四川省地矿局<span lang="EN-US">113</span>地质队高级工程师、技术顾问、水工环地质勘察院总工程师。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年读大学时，开始修炼法轮大法。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，泸州市江阳区四名法轮功学员刘开胜、代群英、简红梅、李世芳到合江县自怀镇赶场，告诉人们法轮大法好，被当地派出所抓捕，随即被合江公安国保刑事拘留，过后关押于泸州市纳溪区看守所。被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，获悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。已被转入四川乐山嘉州监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446721.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/24/446721.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘凯欣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江大兴安岭松岭区法轮功学员，女。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘凯欣在加格达奇打工时，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被警察抓捕，现得知已她被松岭区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早，她被加格达奇看守所送到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁沈阳的维权人士。刘丽是为父亲刘树义劳工权益而上访了十一年。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，时年已经<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁的刘树义为了活命，还在沈阳市苏家屯八一镇政府内烧锅炉，为里面“全心全意为人民服务”的官员做苦力。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">19</span>点，加班的刘树义在上班途中遭遇车祸，按照劳动合同法的规定，用人单位应该以工伤予以补偿，但八一镇政府因为没有为劳动者办理工伤保险，就拒绝承担工伤责任，作为女儿的刘丽开始替父上访维权。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘丽到了北京府右街后被截访送马家楼，然而有沈阳市苏家屯区的截访人员接回。后遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刘丽因“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”被检察院批捕。暂无案件后续信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘丽杰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span><span lang="EN-US"> </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江佳木斯市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生于黑龙江省佳木斯市，毕业于东北师范大学生物系，在佳木斯市职教集团职业学院学报编辑部任职（该职业学院的前身是佳木斯市教育学院）。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年她开始修炼法轮功，连年被学院评为优秀教师。刘丽杰于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被当地国保警察抓捕，后以“取保候审”回家。之后，刘丽杰仍被当局构陷到向阳区检察院，法院对她实施期限半年的“监视居住”，在她家的楼旁安了监控摄像头，有便衣警察带车蹲守。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日早上，刘丽杰和家人到派出所索要所谓的“监视居住”通知书时，被带到了法院。法院刑庭庭长宋涛问刘丽杰是否认罪认罚，刘丽杰拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，建设派出所所长和向阳公安分局国保大队长门茂盛来到刘丽杰家，说她写“<span lang="EN-US">3</span>书”（放弃修炼的所谓“保证书”等）的话，检察院和法院的人说了，她的事就会缓下来。刘丽杰仍然拒绝。后遭关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<span lang="EN-US"> ,</span>在没有辩护人出庭、被告人的辩护权没有获得保障的情况下，刘丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘强等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括刘强在内的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">扶余市五家站东荒村居民，男，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被警察抓捕构陷，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日遭判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年刑期，被送吉林监狱关押。到监狱不久，刘庆被迫害得了脑血栓，曾经<span lang="EN-US">1</span>度卧床不起入住公安医院，家属曾办理保外就医未果，后来病情有所好转，但走路需要两人搀扶才能缓缓移动。自从<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年以来，监狱以疫情为借口，拒绝家属会见，现在刘庆身体具体怎么样，家属很是担忧又焦急。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451703.html#22118211148-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省铁岭市清河区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，多次被迫害，被非法拘留、非法劳教、两次被非法判刑（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年），累计非法刑期达<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年之多。她遭吊铐、电击、冻等惨无人道的折磨，曾经在马三家劳教所被摧残精神失常。刘庆香<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在市场讲真相时，被清河区公安分局国保大抓捕、并抄家。刘庆香被关押在铁岭市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月份被清河区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘庆余：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市大石桥市法轮功学员刘庆余，，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十日，中共江泽民团伙开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，刘庆余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次被中共人员抓捕、劳教、判刑，曾在公安局、看守所、劳教所遭受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，刘庆余被不明真相的人恶意举报，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刘庆余和妻子张畅被抓捕。刘庆余遭刑讯逼供，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被关押在大石桥看守所。妻子张畅被关押到营口市看守所，第<span lang="EN-US">38</span>天被释放。营口市站前区法院通知律师于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午在大石桥市看守所庭审。刘庆余被营口市站前区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/24/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%88%98%E5%BA%86%E4%BD%99%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-433960.html"><b lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘仁秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市旅顺法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前被关押在大连市监狱第五监区。据悉，监狱非法剥夺了他家人的探视权。家人已经有约半年多的时间没有见到他了。刘仁秋是在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被特警在其租住房内抓捕。当天，大连政法委策划，采用手机监控、跟踪、定位、蹲坑等手段，在大连地区各县区同一时间统一行动，抓捕了数十名法轮功学员，有很多人当天被放回，有的当月回家，最后还有多人被判刑。这次抓捕被公安国保称为“<span lang="EN-US">1614</span>”大案。刘仁秋、盛杰、谷树春、王红玉四名法轮功学员，被旅顺法院二次非法开完庭后，在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下判决书， 刘仁秋被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、罚款五万元；盛杰<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半、罚款三万元；王红玉<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚金款三千。刘仁秋刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年的<span lang="EN-US">85</span>岁的法轮功学员瞿月仙与<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁刘荣仙，因为<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份在一起读法轮功著作《转法轮》，分别被昆明市西山区法院判刑，瞿月仙一年六个月，勒索罚金八千元；刘荣仙判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金一万元。刘荣仙刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘瑞莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; lang="EN-US">20</span>多年的迫害中，刘瑞莲曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、劳教两次：<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年（提前释放）；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年再次被劳教（勒索<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元，劳教两年）。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚在家里被抓捕，抢走复印机、电脑、电视、<span lang="EN-US">VCD</span>等。关押<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。这一次是<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日在家中被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日送石家庄女子监狱<span lang="EN-US">14</span>监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐山市玉田县法轮功学员。家住唐山市玉田县窝洛沽镇贾言庄村，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日早晨<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/16/451981.html#22111520446-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/16/451981.html#22111520446-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘淑萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：黑龙江大庆市杜蒙县法轮功学员。一九六三年九月九日出生，今年五十九岁，蒙族，是下岗民办教师，现住黑龙江省大庆市杜蒙县。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因为坚持修炼法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年期间，刘淑萍几次被大庆市局国保和杜蒙县国保便衣警察抓捕，将她构陷到让胡路区检察院、让胡路区法院，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/12/2022-6-12.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/12/2022-6-12.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘淑亚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，原贵阳市铁路客运段退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，贺云杰和刘淑娅为了帮助市民了解法轮功，发放法轮功资料，期间被人恶告。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，贺云杰和刘淑娅分别被贵阳铁路公安、南明区分局国保、二戈寨派出所警察抓捕、抄家，被关押到五当区三江看守所。被关押了<span lang="EN-US">162</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日分别被南宁区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘嗣祖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁夏银川市隆德县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。刘嗣祖因坚持法轮信仰，多年来遭到中共人员的各种迫害：他曾两次被中共法院判刑：<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被隆德县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被银川市兴庆区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午，刘嗣祖在外出时被警察抓捕，随后派出所警察和国保人员闯到他家中抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，刘嗣祖被银川市兴庆区公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中旬，传出刘嗣祖被银川市西夏区法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450330.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450330.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘素芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省鞍山市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，家住辽宁省鞍山市铁西区铁西九道街，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年末开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，刘素芝在立山区太平早市，向过往的人讲述法轮功遭迫害真相，被人恶意举报，随后被曙光派出所警察抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日得知刘素芝被立山法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450329.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:
