style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢永良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南岳阳市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，卢永良在家中与几位法轮功学员一起读法轮大法著作。被警察入户抓捕，并抄家。电脑、打印机、刻录机、大法书籍、真相资料等私人物品被警察抄走。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。卢永良被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被湖南省平江县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，没收电脑、打印机、刻录机、装订机等。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢志英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：卢志英被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陆大新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">长春法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，又名陆大欣、陆方兰。早年修炼法轮大法后，按真、善、忍标准做好人，身心受益。一九九九年，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，她曾三次被抓捕、两次被劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陆大新（陆方兰）被吉林警察抓捕，一直被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，陆大新被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已经转至吉林女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/8/452868.html#22127203045-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/8/452868.html#22127203045-1</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆辉煌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，壮族，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，户籍所在地：广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡上瑶村方和屯<span lang="EN-US">94</span>号。曾在广东珠三角等地工作，工作之余关心国家、民生状况，进行写作并在网络上传播。<span lang="EN-US">2013 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 10 </span>月，其写了《致中共中央公开信——关于政治体制改革的思考和建议》，在文中分析了国家的政治体制并建议中共中央进行宪政改革<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月，其写了《“妄议”国事》一文，在文中批评了个别国家领导人和政策。<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 6 </span>月，其写下《致习近平总书记的公开信》，呼吁习近平关注、关心农民工。以上三篇文章只是在一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群和一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>好友中传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1 </span>月，其写了《对当前政局的分析与呼吁》，在文中分析了当时的时局，反对修宪和个人崇拜，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信、邮箱传播，并向《北京之春》网站投稿，《北京之春》网站分别于<span lang="EN-US"> 2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">25 </span>日和<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 28 </span>日分上篇和下篇刊登了该文。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7 </span>月，其写作《“艰时克共”的建议》，呼吁早日促进《零八宪章》的目标实现，并通过微信群传播，后又在《北京之春》网站刊登。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>月，其写了《致“中国劳工观察”组织的信》，在文中描述了中国劳工特别是农民工的真实情况，并请求“中国劳工观察”组织帮助他们维权，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信，向朋友传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其在深圳富士康鸿观厂区被深圳市龙华区公安分局福民派出所传唤到该派出所。（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在签刑事拘留通知书时，其知道并没有人报案，他们是根据上级部门监控发现深圳有人传播所谓政治不当言论的线索，并依据文章的线索传唤。）在派出所里，警察在还没立案（也就是说还没进入刑事阶段）之前，就利用威胁（不说就打）手段获取其手机、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱等密码，并利用这些密码非法登录其<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱，搜集其所谓犯罪证据。就这样，公安机关在其手机便签、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱搜集到了前面其所列举的六篇文章。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，公安机关以这六篇文章作为证据开始立案，将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日将其逮捕，之后经过两次退回补充侦查，三次延长审查起诉。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，深圳市龙华检察院以所谓的散布虚假信息、辱骂国家领导人、造谣污蔑国家的政治体制、法律制度、基本国策、指导思想、战略布局、反腐斗争、发展路线、劳工制度与现状、民族复兴目标等，涉嫌寻衅滋事罪起诉，所谓的罪证就是其前面列举的六篇文章。由于其坚持不认罪，并在里面坚持斗争，遭遇了杨伟东恶警施加的电击、禁食、戴镣铐等酷刑。并且不准其与家人通信。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日（接到起诉书的第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天），在深圳市龙华法院开庭前会议，就证据的合法性进行质疑。由于家人没有给其请律师，其律师是官派的，在这次庭前会议上根本没有就证据的合法性为其辩护。而陆辉煌本人就检方的证据提出三个疑点：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、其写的文章属于言论自由的范畴。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、检方的证据是利用非法手段（威胁手段）取得的。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、检方指控其在《北京之春》刊发文章，也是通过翻墙的手段获得的，根据《宪法》人人平等的原则，公检法等机关并没有特权，他们能用的，咱们平民百姓也能用。他们能翻墙，咱平民百姓也能翻墙，那就没有必要浪费大量纳税人的钱去建所谓的“防火墙”了。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在深圳市龙华法院正式开庭。其本人写的辩护词不让其带到法庭。在上车去法庭时，法警给其戴上头套，只露出眼睛，到了法院才摘下来。在庭审时，审判长江涛以不准辱骂国家领导人为由阻止其为自己辩护。庭审只用了大约一个小时就草草结束。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其接到判决书，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，由于在看守所长期睡地板，导致其得了风湿，腰椎疾病。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被调往广东省从化监狱服刑，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日刑满释放。释放后多次申诉无果。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点，广西异议人士陆辉煌在南宁市大岭新村居住地被多名不明身份男子带走。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，朋友拨打不通陆辉煌电话，致电陆辉煌户籍所在地广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡派出所询问，接线员否认有抓陆辉煌，但言语闪烁其词。陆辉煌曾因言论获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月刑满释放。有网友猜测陆辉煌被再次带走，或与其签名呼吁彻查徐州铁链女奴事件有关。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，陆辉煌被广西壮族自治区贵港市法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日；其不服，已表示上诉。目前被羁押于广西贵港市看守所（广西壮族自治区贵港市港南区八塘镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">537131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_19.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_19.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陆建华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，上海市人，前中国最高层核心智囊之一，第二届“北京市十大杰出青年”，曾任中国社会科学院社会学研究所研究员、公共政策研究中心副主任，中央电视台特约评论员和重庆市渝北区副区长等职，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，因陆续为香港记者程翔提供<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余篇稿件，其中<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月所提供的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>篇文章内容被中共视为涉及“国家绝密资料”，遂于<span lang="EN-US"> 2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被国家安全局秘密拘捕；后经秘密审判，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市第二中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 20</span>年；其上诉坚称自己被冤，均被驳回。目前在北京市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆建荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏讨薪农民工、维权公民。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年先后两次于六四敏感日因转发中国公民及国际友人在驻美中国大使馆门口举行纪念“六<span lang="EN-US">.</span>四”活动的图片遭到警方传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被江苏警方跨省抓捕，涉嫌“非法买卖枪支弹药罪”，至今不被释放，被刑拘于泰兴市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">鲁•贡确嘉措：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海省黄南州尖扎县拉莫德钦寺僧人，因写书记录流亡印度觐见达赖喇嘛尊者的经历，近日第二次遭当局带走，目前与外界失联。鲁•贡确嘉措将自己翻越雪山、赴印拜见达赖喇嘛尊者的过程，写成名为《五十四天》的书籍。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年年底完稿后被警方约谈，带到黄南州国安局非法扣留审问长达一周之久，并被警告不得出版该书。获释后不满一个月，贡确嘉措再次被当局约谈，目前与外界失联。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，黄南州统战部打电话约谈，他回复说等雪停了后再去，结果下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分左右，两名黄南州安全局的人员将他带走，之后便没有了任何消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">鲁孟君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（鲁梦军、鲁梦君）女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，湖南省湘潭市法轮功学员。家住湖南省湘潭市护潭乡繁城村向荣组，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年下半年走上修炼法轮功之路。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，鲁孟君曾两次被判刑，每次判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，共<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年冤狱，在湖南省女子监狱遭受酷刑体罚折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，鲁孟君被湘潭市雨湖区公安分局警察抓捕、抄家，关押在湘潭市看守所，不准家人见面，在家人不知任何情况之下，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日第三次被劫入湖南省女子监狱。据悉鲁孟君被判刑七年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">鲁扬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，本名张桂祺，网名“鲁西狂徒”，山东省莘县人，著名诗人。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年开始诗歌文学创作活动，创办“扬子宛诗社”，并主编出版《扬子宛诗刊》。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年创办“中国当代诗歌论坛”，出版主编《中国当代诗歌》刊物。二年后“中国当代诗论坛”被封。期间开始在《星星》、《诗选刊》等国内著名诗歌刊物上发表诗歌。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年创办“中国自由文化论坛”，因颇有影响而被迫多次关停，后移入外网“自由中国”网站，最后又移入博讯网站。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年因自由写作被迫于聊城外国学校辞职，后妻子工作也受到牵连，一起离开山东，南方谋生，此间由诗歌创作转入文化自由写作，大量作品发表于国内各大网站，并被海外多家网站转载。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年参与“零八宪章”签署，夫妻工作再次受到影响，双双失业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，为支持入狱的本会前会长刘晓波而入独立中文笔会。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年受“茉莉花运动”影响，再次失业并遭遣返回山东老家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因举牌声援批评毛泽东遭解职的山东广播电视台特约评论员邓相超教授，在邓教授所在的济南建筑大学遭到暴徒殴打，受到中外媒体关注，同时也成为有关部门重点监控对象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年创办“中国诗人大讲堂——文殊书院”，继续从事自由文化传播事业。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方带走，下落不明近两个星期，后被聊城市公安局以“涉嫌颠覆国家政权罪”宣布刑事拘留，后遭正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日已被秘密开庭，家属竟然被封锁，对此一无所知。关押于聊城市看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日获悉，鲁扬先生被聊城中级法院重判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/6_26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/6_26.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">栾长辉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁葫芦岛市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">葫芦岛市渤海造船厂工程师。栾长辉<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在上班时，被龙港区边防派出所所长孙玉柱等抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被连山区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日家属接到葫芦岛市连山区法院的判决书，栾长辉被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，他被押入辽宁省沈阳第一监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E6%A0%BE%E9%95%BF%E8%BE%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434545.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/9/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E8%91%AB%E8%8A%A6%E5%B2%9B%E5%B8%82%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%B8%88%E6%A0%BE%E9%95%BF%E8%BE%89%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434545.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">栾凝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，大学文化，原来在宁夏劳动人事厅工作，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功前，是宁夏法轮功辅导站副站长（义务教功）。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，栾凝到兴庆区一邮政储蓄所邮寄信件。栾凝离开后，被该所人员以信件涉及法轮功内容向派出所报警，并将信件交给派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，栾凝上班时在家门口被抓捕。宁夏银川市中级法院在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下达判决书，对栾凝判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛迪嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区索县若达乡索卡村人，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Lodoe Gyamtso</span>，西藏民间舞蹈艺术家，藏族人权捍卫者，异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代初，曾因其姐、妹二人在一场车祸中被司机撞死及遭到谋杀，而当时的那曲地方法院竟枉法以该司机为亲共藏人为由，判其“无罪”；同年晚些时候，两人在村庄市场相遇，随发生争执冲突，冲突中为了躲避司机方对其的两次射杀，其被迫自卫，刺伤了司机，致使该司机虽送医院仍最终死亡；针此，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被西藏那曲中级法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后送拉萨市扎奇监狱服刑；服刑期间，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又曾因在扎奇监狱带领狱友高喊“西藏独立”，“中国退出西藏”，“祈愿达赖喇嘛尊者长久住世”，“六百万藏人要团结”等口号进行抗议，并散发手写传单<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多份，在遭受审讯及酷刑折磨<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月之后，被西藏当局决定处于死刑，后在联合国及国际特赦等组织的干预下，才未对其施行处决，但又加刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并被转至拉萨市曲水监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其终获刑满获释，但又被软禁在家<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，曾因公开谴责中共西藏当局强迫居住在西藏巴青县、索县和比如县的藏人中共八一建军节时穿珍贵野兽皮毛饰品（此为传统藏人服饰，但藏人已从<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年始自愿放弃穿戴该饰品）和表演歌舞等，并将其认同的达赖喇嘛提出的解决西藏问题的“中间道路”和“和平区”等概念，以及对佛教姻缘和非暴力原则重要性的感悟和认识，让其妻噶吉拍录视频，广为传播，而遭致当局的仇视与严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又曾因公开反对中共当局强令除在西藏之外，在藏区其他各地寺院里学习的僧侣、尼师必须限期返回索县和比如县等，否则其家属将面临遭监禁和接受禁止挖虫草处罚等非人道作法（挖虫草是当地藏人经济收入的最主要来源），随再遭当局拘押，并关押在比如县监狱中，后因健康状况不佳，才准予释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因在拉萨市布达拉宫前举行抗议活动，并在网上发视频，宣称自己正在发起一场“世界和平运动”，引起海外流亡藏人广泛热议，随被那曲地区索县警方再次拘捕，并被以“国家机密案”论处；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，其被西藏自治区那曲县中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”再次重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前在拉萨市扎什监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑慈诚（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，藏族良心犯。洛桑慈诚和洛桑祥曲两名年轻僧人于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底被当地警方从格尔登寺院抓走后，长达<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月一直没有任何消息。他们被当局指控涉嫌与自焚僧人扎白事件有关。洛桑慈诚，是阿坝县求吉玛乡人，当年<span lang="EN-US">19</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬被当局秘密（没有通知家属情况下）判处<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑丹增（藏<span lang="EN-US">/</span>左贡寺高僧）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年左右出生，西藏自治区昌都市左贡县旺达镇乌雅村人，又称乌雅•朱古（即转世喇嘛）洛桑丹增仁波切，早年曾在阿里地区任职导游和司机，后成为西藏左贡寺高僧。曾因经常到西藏的左贡县左贡寺劝导僧俗民众停止供奉所谓的“朵杰凶天”，而要为西藏民族的长远理想和第十四世达赖喇嘛的健康长寿着想，并鼓励藏人努力保护、发扬民族宗教与文化等，受到藏人僧俗的广泛爱戴和尊敬，随招致中共当局的恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在西藏拉萨市被左贡县警方抓走刑拘，后被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月初，被西藏自治区左贡县法院以“追随达赖分裂集团”、“劝诫、蛊惑地方藏民停止修供凶天”等为罪由，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑格培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">2016</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡第二大队人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，曾因政治诉求于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被当局抓捕并被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，至<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被提前数月释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，其直到一个月前仍处于下落不明状态，且当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑克珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">现年<span lang="EN-US">44</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县贾柯河牧场人，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。自幼进入格尔登寺为僧，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因政治诉求被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后因当时在狱中受虐严重，导致罹患重病而被提前释放，后经由家人、亲友自筹经费，让其住院长时治疗，才得以转危为安。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被警方突然从其僧舍带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其因被指控涉嫌“在微信建立组群为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿，特别收集长寿祈愿文持诵及持咒数量”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑桑杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，青海省果洛州久治县人，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺（又译格德寺）僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因向外透露格尔登寺僧人自焚抗议事件真相，而被中共当地警方抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并被追加指控涉嫌制作、出售达赖喇嘛的相片和讲法的影片等，违法了中国法律，遂于当年被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日秘密获释；据悉，其在狱中因遭受酷刑虐待，以致出狱时身体状况极差，出现丧失记忆症状；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其再次被当地警方以涉嫌藏人自焚抗议等“政治问题”抓捕、刑拘；在非法关押长达<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月之后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院一审以“政治问题”（不知名罪名）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日；因当地对藏族群体高压严控情况十分严重，故其具体情况缺详。目前其羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县安斗乡克洼村人，当地知名画家东阔之子，原格尔登寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因政治诉求而被当局抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被警方带走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而被拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗纯贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">抚顺市望花区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁的罗纯贵老人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在古城子第<span lang="EN-US">8</span>中学附近讲真相，被警察抓捕，由于疫情，回家被监视居住。古城子派出所警察经常到他家骚扰，后来望花检察院也去骚扰，对罗纯贵起诉，罗纯贵被迫流离失所。警察还经常到家找他儿子骚扰，他儿子不配合，拒绝回答。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，罗纯贵去建设市场时被电子眼拍到，被抓捕到建设派出所，后被望花法院秘密开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。现被关押抚顺看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/9/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%BD%97%E7%BA%AF%E8%B4%B5%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430595.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/9/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%8A%9A%E9%A1%BA%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E7%BD%97%E7%BA%AF%E8%B4%B5%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%98%E5%AF%86%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-430595.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗建荣：</span></b><a name="_Hlk52322614"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省南城县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生。</span></a><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省南城县洪门镇付前村人。罗建荣从<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始修炼至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，在修炼不到十年的时间，曾经被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗江英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，广东省湛江市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代生人，广东湛江人，原中山大学附属第三医院（中山三院）的护士，一九九九年二月开始修炼法轮功，在中共对法轮功持续至今逾二十一年的迫害中，这是罗江英女士被中共绑架、关押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次。罗江英女士曾经被劳教两年、关洗脑班一年、被判刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，她在广东湛江某市场宣传法轮功被恶人绑架，晚上被警察抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年中国新年前，被湛江市赤坎区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，目前，被关押在遂溪县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">罗立腾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北麻城法轮功学员。罗立腾系麻城市中驿镇方河村人。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，他们受到骚扰、迫害。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，罗立腾曾于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因修炼法轮功被中共判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，在沙洋范家台监狱受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，他在外打工回家休假几天，期间正赶上法轮功创始人李大师生日，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日这天，当地修炼法轮功的乡亲们，有十几人不约而同地来到罗家，然后顺理成章地给大法师父拜寿，谁知他去外地打工途中，在麻城火车北站被查出手机上拍下的此内容，即被麻城铁路派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中旬，罗立腾被麻城市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/28/450170.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/28/450170.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗明春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川西昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，被国安抓捕控制后抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗其刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省淮南市人，强拆受害者，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。因其所在淮南市山南新区合法住宅遭政府强拆，并且长期不予合法安置补偿，故多次向有关部门依法投诉、求助而无果，后其被迫经常进京上访维权；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因在北京一边打工一边信访过程中，在抖音上发了一条反映其维权真实情况的视频，遂很快被网警发现，并被安徽维稳人员紧急遣返原籍，并于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被淮南市山南新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，又快速被淮南市大通区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；维权友人疑指，其被逮捕可能与中共“二十大”召开维稳有关。目前被羁押于淮南市看守所（安徽省淮南市田家庵区安成镇黑泥村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">232001</span>）。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_55.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_55.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗巧俐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省攀枝花市法轮功学员。从湖南来父母家探亲的罗巧俐和妹妹罗巧萍，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在攀枝花市西区清香坪向世人发疫情刊物等法轮功资料时，被人诬告。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金。罗巧俐刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗巧萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省攀枝花市法轮功学员。从湖南来父母家探亲的罗巧俐和妹妹罗巧萍，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在攀枝花市西区清香坪向世人发疫情刊物等法轮功资料时，被人诬告。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金。罗巧萍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">罗让贡求（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，格尔登寺僧人、中国在押良心犯。曾因与境外藏族流亡组织“格尔底寺新闻联络小组”成员三木旦保持联系，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月起又因藏区出现自焚抗争浪潮，格尔登寺年轻僧人扎白等人在此亦以自焚行动向中共当局对藏区长期实施高压严控政策表达强烈不满与抗争，其为让外界获此消息，随将扎白等自焚者的身份、背景等信息发给流亡印度的藏人组织，引起中共当局的强烈不满；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因四川省阿坝县再次发生多起藏人自焚抗争事件，随引起中共高层的极度恐慌和严酷打压；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其被四川省阿坝县警方以“煽动自焚杀人”罪名抓捕刑拘，并被指控“利用其格西身份，在众僧侣中大肆鼓动自焚，单独或伙同被告人罗让才让在阿坝县物色自焚人员，先后煽动、引诱、教唆或者胁迫多人自焚死亡，并将自焚的相关信息提供给境外组织，以使他们用此进行分裂活动”；后被当地警方正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，缓期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年执行，剥夺政治权利终身。目前疑似在四川省阿坝监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_19.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_19.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗桑金巴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">Lobsang Jinpa</span>，西藏自治区日喀则市定日县人，藏族僧侣，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏民称之为登卓寺（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>））副院长，公益慈善捐助人，藏族异见人士，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，曾因当卓寺僧侣曲嘉旺波（<span lang="EN-US">Choegyal Wangpo</span>）到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时不慎将手机丢失，后被当地警方获取，发现手机里存有其及当卓寺的多名僧侣与尼泊尔的同乡藏僧有过密联系的信息记录，尤其是针对<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震，他们向那里的藏人及寺院捐款，以帮助地震灾区小区重建等记录，以及存有和第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛有关的图片及文献等，遂引起中共西藏当局的极大不快和恐慌，认定这是一起与境外敌对势力勾结，利用在线通讯对国家安全构成威胁的典型案件；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，罗桑金巴所在当卓寺遭到日喀则市当局派出的多名武警及公安警察突袭，所有僧人均被强迫接受政治洗脑教育，多人遭殴打，包含其在内的<span lang="EN-US">20</span>名僧侣均被拘留，所在区域的网络连接被切断；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天后，一名僧人因向当局抗议而自杀，其及多名僧人仍被超押，数月不放；后罗桑金巴与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名藏僧被日喀则市警方以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由转正式逮捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其一行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案在日喀则中级法院庭审，最终被以“危害国家安全罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>年不等刑期；其中，罗桑金巴被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_53.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_53.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗太会：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。罗太会刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">罗晓星：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省攀枝花市法轮功学员。从湖南来父母家探亲的罗巧俐和妹妹罗巧萍，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在攀枝花市西区清香坪向世人发疫情刊物等法轮功资料时，被人诬告。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，罗巧俐和罗巧萍同时在各自的居住处被抓捕。因为全家修炼法轮功，一直和父母住在一起的弟弟罗晓星及母亲也同时被抓捕。一直被关押在仁和区棉纱湾看守所。姐弟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日两次被开庭，后获悉，罗巧俐、罗巧萍、罗晓星分别诬判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金。罗晓星刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗新平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁夏银川市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，系宁夏银川市金凤区退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，罗新平去小百货店买东西，告诉店里那个人，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”，瘟疫来时，能保命、保平安。谁知那人恶意向公安告发。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">结果，罗新平女士被银川市兴庆区公安分局国保警察抓捕。后被批捕、起诉、开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日， 罗新平的家属和辩护律师在接到了宁夏回族自治区银川市西夏区法院判决书，罗新平被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金两万元。被关押在银川市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，罗新平被关押到宁夏女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">骆元英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，女，家住武汉市新天门墩。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月骆元英修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，骆元英多次被关看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱迫害，遭到各种酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午十点左右，骆元英、黄红卫在武汉市江岸区三眼桥附近给民众讲真相时遭人恶告，被江汉区国保大队、唐家墩派出所警察抓捕。两人被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。而在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日拘留结束当日，两人被转为刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，江汉区检察院对骆元英、黄红蔚下达批捕书；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月上旬将两人构陷到汉阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被汉阳法院判刑，骆元英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元；黄红蔚被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。骆元英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕春钰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，辽宁省大连法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">一名乡村医生，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，行医<span lang="EN-US">4</span>。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年了，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年开始修炼法轮大法，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共集团开始迫害法轮功以后，吕春钰因为坚持自己的信仰，告诉人们法轮功被迫害的真相，屡次被抓捕、骚扰迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，吕春钰家属找律师去大连姚家看守所会见吕春钰，律师说：吕春钰已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，最近要送到监狱去，现在不让会见。现羁押在大连姚家看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/4/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E5%90%95%E6%98%A5%E9%92%B0%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E9%9B%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-439636.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/4/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E8%80%81%E5%A4%AA%E5%90%95%E6%98%A5%E9%92%B0%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E9%9B%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88-439636.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吕耿松：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1956</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，浙江省杭州市人，前浙江省高等公安专科学校教师，独立撰稿人，中国民主党浙江委员会重要成员，人权活动家，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日因言获罪被抄家拘捕，并被羁押于浙江省杭州市西湖看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，被杭州市中级人民法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日刑满获释。出狱后因仍持守民主理念，关注民主宪政建设，帮助访民维权，遂遭到中共当局严密监控和恶意打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被杭州市警方抄家、传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被杭州市警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被杭州市检察院转正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被杭州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬经浙江省杭州市高级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判。目前在浙江省湖州市长湖监狱服刑。吕耿松目前在狱中身体状况极差，不仅被诊断有胆囊坏死，而且有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>颗牙齿牙髓坏死，不能进食。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其亲友前去探监，发现其比之前身体更为虚弱，当地气候虽早已入春，但其身上仍穿着棉袄、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>件加绒内衣、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>条加厚保暖裤和头戴御寒的帽子，还感觉寒冷，并言称“怕风怕冷已很长时间”，“剩下的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年多刑期恐熬不过去了”；其曾多次申请保外就医，但一直遭拒。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕国妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕国妹是上海浦东新区唐镇前进村西李家宅<span lang="EN-US">202</span>号吕湘福的女儿，他家的合法私有房屋在家庭人员坚守在屋顶护家园抗强拆<span lang="EN-US">6</span>天<span lang="EN-US">5</span>夜半，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">12</span>时许被中共政府强拆。参与护家园抗强拆的今年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的吕湘福，<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚上被警察带走，同时被带走的另外<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名屋顶抗争者都下落不明。后吕国妹的家属收到《拘留通知书》才知道吕国妹已于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日<span lang="EN-US">19</span>：<span lang="EN-US">55</span>分被上海市公安局浦东分局以“拒不执行判决罪”为名刑事拘留，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕丽珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林长春法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕丽珍<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午被西安广场派出所抓捕、抄家。随后<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，吕丽珍被安广场派出所关押到长春第四看守所关押，后被批捕、构陷朝阳区检察院。吕丽珍<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被长春市朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被关押到吉林省女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451694.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451694.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕梅霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京昌平区法轮功学员，家住北京昌平南口采石场宿舍。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午在家被北京警察抓捕，被关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月得知她被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/24/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%98%8C%E5%B9%B3%E5%8C%BA%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%95%E6%A2%85%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-441654.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/24/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%98%8C%E5%B9%B3%E5%8C%BA%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E5%90%95%E6%A2%85%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-441654.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕世瑜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1999</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，香港籍人，香港新界东部粉岭公民，理工大学土木工程系学生，“自由香港”追求者，香港反送中运动支持者，<span lang="EN-US">Telegram</span>频道「抗共港独台<span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;H.K.I.A.F</span>」管理员，中国在押政治犯。自幼生活于小康之家，深得父母之爱，后因其父早逝，随与其母、其姐艰难度日；又因自小患有多动症（又即过度活跃症），注意力难以专注学业，故而其中学毕业后未能及时升读大学，后经克服困难，终于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年入读香港理工大学土木工程系；然而就在此刻，香港发生了举世瞩目的反送中大游行，其因与众多香港市民及大学生积极反对中共当权者在香港全面实施《逃犯条例修订草案》，以及深刻经历了香港市民在抗议行动中遭到前所未有的港警及中共专程调配入港的大规模军警的极端镇压，随其为了捍卫香港的真民主、真自由，自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日起，以自家住所作为武器库，收藏胡椒球弹及大量气枪装备等物品，并在<span lang="EN-US">facebook</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Instagram&nbsp;</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Telegram</span>上售卖武器及发表所谓“港独”和宣扬仇恨的言论；后因其言行被香港警方获悉，于同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其母子二人统一被香港粉岭警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌“违反《港区国安法》落实罪”移送给香港国安处接手调查；之后，其母子均以涉嫌“无牌管有枪械及弹药”、“未经许可输入战略物品”和“藏有攻击性武器”三罪被起诉；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其母被准予保释，但其仍被香港屯门裁判法院首次提堂；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，又被粉岭法院二度提堂受审，未果。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其被西九龙法院再次庭审，被指因于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日之间，“在香港煽动他人组织、策划、实施或者参与实施旨在分裂国家、破坏国家统一行为，不论是否使用武力或者以武力相威胁，即将香港特别行政区从中华人民共和国分离出去或非法改变香港特别行政区的法律地位，被加控一项《港区国安法》中的煽动他人分裂国家罪，而原有的无牌进口战略物品罪则不再提控”；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案又在香港区域法院被提堂庭审，原定欲判其有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，但法官获控方提醒，指其因主张「港独」呼吁人们武装起来革命，<span lang="EN-US">Telegram</span>频道公开，提出能出售武器装备供人攻击或自卫之用，遂违反《港区国安法》情节严重，需要加刑，故而最终被香港高级法院以“煽动他人分裂国家罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前服刑监狱不详，或仍羁押于荔枝角收押所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5_16.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5_16.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕相富：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：吕相富</span>被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年；<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕月霞与赵文静、黄金桔、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。后所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。该教会成立于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size:
